<div style="border: 2px solid #484898; background: #FFF; padding: 1ex 1ex 1ex 1.5ex; margin: 0px 0px 10px 0px; font-size: 90%">
<div style="border-bottom: 2px dotted #484898; font-size: 110%"><b>Arts and Entertainment Work Group</b></div>
<p>The Arts and Entertainment Work Group is a working group of members of the Biography WikiProject dedicated to ensuring quality and coverage of biography articles.</p>

<p><br /></p>
<div style="border-bottom: 2px dotted #484898; margin-top:5px;"><b>Related Projects</b></div>
<p>Since biographies are potentially under the purview of almost all WikiProjects, it is important that we work in tandem with these projects. Also, when seeking collaboration on articles, don't neglect to approach WikiProjects that are part of the geographical region your subject is/was in.</p>
<div style="border-bottom: 2px dotted #484898; margin-top:5px;"><b>Related Portals</b></div>
<p>Increase the exposure of our work group by nominating our articles for their Portal FA and DYKs... Specific discipline portals are listed in that section.</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Portal:Arts" title="Portal:Arts">Portal:Arts</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Portal:Geography" title="Portal:Geography">Portal:Geography</a> - to browse for a region in case the bio is a good candidate for a regional portal</li>
</ul>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Directions_for_expanding_any_division_below">Directions for expanding any division below</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:WikiProject_Biography/Arts_and_entertainment&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Directions for expanding any division below">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:WikiProject_Biography/Arts_and_entertainment&amp;veaction=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Directions for expanding any division below" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The general outline and collection has been started, but if you would like to expand and organize a discipline, here's what you do. Right below the page heading for the discipline insert this: {{subst:<a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Biography/Work_groups/Division_banner" title="Wikipedia:WikiProject Biography/Work groups/Division banner">Wikipedia:WikiProject Biography/Work groups/Division banner</a>}} and save. This will put a rough outline together for you and then you can edit it to conform to your area. See <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Biography/Arts_and_entertainment#Writers_and_critics" title="Wikipedia:WikiProject Biography/Arts and entertainment">Writers and critics</a> below for an example. If your project grows large enough where it's taking up a good portion of this page, you should probably move it to a subpage of this page.</p>
<p>You might also want to make a Members section for people to join your specific area!</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Tagging_articles">Tagging articles</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:WikiProject_Biography/Arts_and_entertainment&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Tagging articles">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:WikiProject_Biography/Arts_and_entertainment&amp;veaction=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Tagging articles" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Any article related to this work group should be marked by adding <code style="white-space:nowrap;">|a&amp;e-work-group=yes</code> to the {{<a href="/wiki/Template:WPBiography" title="Template:WPBiography" class="mw-redirect">WPBiography</a>}} project banner at the top of its talk page. This will automatically place it into <a href="/wiki/Category:Arts_and_entertainment_work_group_articles" title="Category:Arts and entertainment work group articles">Category:Arts and entertainment work group articles</a>. Articles can be assessed for priority within this work group by using the <code style="white-space:nowrap;">|a&amp;e-priority=</code> parameter. See <a href="/wiki/Template:WPBiography/doc" title="Template:WPBiography/doc" class="mw-redirect">Template:WPBiography/doc</a> for detailed instructions on how to use the banner.</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Gregor_Laubsch"><a href="/wiki/Gregor_Laubsch" title="Gregor Laubsch">Gregor Laubsch</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Gregor_Laubsch&amp;action=edit&amp;section=T-1" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Gregor Laubsch">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Gregor_Laubsch&amp;veaction=edit&amp;section=T-1" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Gregor Laubsch" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl>
<dd><span id="Gregor_Laubsch"></span><span class="plainlinks nourlexpansion lx"><a href="/wiki/Gregor_Laubsch" title="Gregor Laubsch">Gregor Laubsch</a> <tt>(</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Gregor_Laubsch&amp;action=edit">edit</a><tt>|</tt><a href="/wiki/Talk:Gregor_Laubsch" title="Talk:Gregor Laubsch">talk</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Gregor_Laubsch&amp;action=history">history</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Gregor_Laubsch&amp;action=protect">protect</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Whatlinkshere/Gregor_Laubsch&amp;limit=999">links</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Gregor_Laubsch&amp;action=watch">watch</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;page=Gregor+Laubsch">logs</a><tt>)</tt></span> – (<a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Gregor_Laubsch" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Gregor Laubsch">View AfD</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://toolserver.org/~snottywong/cgi-bin/votecounter.cgi?page=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Gregor_Laubsch">Stats</a></span>)</dd>
<dd>(<span class="plainlinks" style=""><i>Find sources:</i>&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?as_eq=wikipedia&amp;q=%22Gregor+Laubsch%22&amp;num=50">"Gregor Laubsch"</a>&#160;–&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?q=%22Gregor+Laubsch%22&amp;tbm=nws&amp;tbs=ar:1">news</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?tbs=bks:1&amp;q=%22Gregor+Laubsch%22">books</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://scholar.google.com/scholar?q=%22Gregor+Laubsch%22">scholar</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.jstor.org/action/doBasicSearch?Query=%22Gregor+Laubsch%22&amp;acc=on&amp;wc=on">JSTOR</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://images.google.com/images?safe=off&amp;as_rights=(cc_publicdomain%7ccc_attribute%7ccc_sharealike%7ccc_noncommercial%7ccc_nonderived)&amp;q=%22Gregor+Laubsch%22">free images</a></span>)</dd>
</dl>
<p>I stand by my claim from the original prod that this fails <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:N" title="Wikipedia:N" class="mw-redirect">notability</a>. All sources seem like regional or specialist magazines, no coverage in mainstream sources. All awards look minor. Nothing to suggest encyclopedic notability that I see so far. <sub style="border:1px solid #228B22;padding:1px;"><a href="/wiki/User:Piotrus" title="User:Piotrus">Piotr Konieczny aka Prokonsul Piotrus</a>| <a href="/wiki/User_talk:Piotrus" title="User talk:Piotrus"><font style="color:#7CFC00;background:#006400;">reply here</font></a></sub> 07:45, 27 August 2013 (UTC)</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Mohamed_Temam"><a href="/wiki/Mohamed_Temam" title="Mohamed Temam">Mohamed Temam</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Mohamed_Temam&amp;action=edit&amp;section=T-1" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Mohamed Temam">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Mohamed_Temam&amp;veaction=edit&amp;section=T-1" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Mohamed Temam" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl>
<dd><span id="Mohamed_Temam"></span><span class="plainlinks nourlexpansion lx"><a href="/wiki/Mohamed_Temam" title="Mohamed Temam">Mohamed Temam</a> <tt>(</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Mohamed_Temam&amp;action=edit">edit</a><tt>|</tt><a href="/wiki/Talk:Mohamed_Temam" title="Talk:Mohamed Temam">talk</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Mohamed_Temam&amp;action=history">history</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Mohamed_Temam&amp;action=protect">protect</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Whatlinkshere/Mohamed_Temam&amp;limit=999">links</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Mohamed_Temam&amp;action=watch">watch</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;page=Mohamed+Temam">logs</a><tt>)</tt></span> – (<a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Mohamed_Temam" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Mohamed Temam">View AfD</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://toolserver.org/~snottywong/cgi-bin/votecounter.cgi?page=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Mohamed_Temam">Stats</a></span>)</dd>
<dd>(<span class="plainlinks" style=""><i>Find sources:</i>&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?as_eq=wikipedia&amp;q=%22Mohamed+Temam%22&amp;num=50">"Mohamed Temam"</a>&#160;–&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?q=%22Mohamed+Temam%22&amp;tbm=nws&amp;tbs=ar:1">news</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?tbs=bks:1&amp;q=%22Mohamed+Temam%22">books</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://scholar.google.com/scholar?q=%22Mohamed+Temam%22">scholar</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.jstor.org/action/doBasicSearch?Query=%22Mohamed+Temam%22&amp;acc=on&amp;wc=on">JSTOR</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://images.google.com/images?safe=off&amp;as_rights=(cc_publicdomain%7ccc_attribute%7ccc_sharealike%7ccc_noncommercial%7ccc_nonderived)&amp;q=%22Mohamed+Temam%22">free images</a></span>)</dd>

<li>As at <a href="/wiki/Hassane_Amraoui" title="Hassane Amraoui">Hassane Amraoui</a>, my comments on which I'm assuming are the reason my participation here was solicited, the big problem is the quality of sources. I just checked each one individually, and here's the rundown: two of them don't actually mention Benyahia's name <i>at all</i>, one is a dead or mistyped link whose content I'm unable to verify at all, and a couple just list his name while containing no actual content about him. Only one link leads to an article that actually uses his name in a larger context, and even that one isn't a particularly <i>substantial</i> article. As always I'm willing to reconsider this if stronger sources start showing up, but we're pretty clearly on the <b>delete</b> side of the see-saw here. <a href="/wiki/User:Bearcat" title="User:Bearcat">Bearcat</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Bearcat" title="User talk:Bearcat">talk</a>) 02:03, 27 August 2013 (UTC)</li>

Wikipedia has <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Policies_and_guidelines" title="Wikipedia:Policies and guidelines">policies and guidelines</a> regarding the encyclopedia's content, and <b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Consensus" title="Wikipedia:Consensus">consensus</a></b> (agreement) is gauged based on the merits of the arguments, <i>not</i> by counting votes.

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Zambranaing"><a href="/wiki/Zambranaing" title="Zambranaing">Zambranaing</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Zambranaing&amp;action=edit&amp;section=T-1" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Zambranaing">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Zambranaing&amp;veaction=edit&amp;section=T-1" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Zambranaing" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl>
<dd><span id="Zambranaing"></span><span class="plainlinks nourlexpansion lx"><a href="/wiki/Zambranaing" title="Zambranaing">Zambranaing</a> <tt>(</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Zambranaing&amp;action=edit">edit</a><tt>|</tt><a href="/w/index.php?title=Talk:Zambranaing&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Talk:Zambranaing (page does not exist)">talk</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Zambranaing&amp;action=history">history</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Zambranaing&amp;action=protect">protect</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Whatlinkshere/Zambranaing&amp;limit=999">links</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Zambranaing&amp;action=watch">watch</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;page=Zambranaing">logs</a><tt>)</tt></span> – (<a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Zambranaing" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Zambranaing">View AfD</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://toolserver.org/~snottywong/cgi-bin/votecounter.cgi?page=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Zambranaing">Stats</a></span>)</dd>

<p>Non-<a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:N" title="Wikipedia:N" class="mw-redirect">notable</a> <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:NEOLOGISM" title="Wikipedia:NEOLOGISM" class="mw-redirect">neologism</a>. <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:MADEUP" title="Wikipedia:MADEUP" class="mw-redirect">Wikipedia is not for things you made up one day</a>. No evidence that this word has any widespread usage. Prod removed without comment by original author. So here we are at AFD. <a href="/wiki/User:WikiDan61" title="User:WikiDan61"><font color="green">WikiDan61</font></a><sup><a href="/wiki/User_talk:WikiDan61" title="User talk:WikiDan61">ChatMe!</a></sup><sub><a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/WikiDan61" title="Special:Contributions/WikiDan61">ReadMe!!</a></sub> 15:57, 23 August 2013 (UTC)</p>

<li><b>Delete</b> Non-notable <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:NEO" title="Wikipedia:NEO" class="mw-redirect">WP:NEO</a>. <a href="/wiki/User:StevenD99" title="User:StevenD99"><font color="#00A" face="High Tower Text"><b>StevenD99</b></font></a> <sup><a href="/wiki/User_talk:StevenD99#top" title="User talk:StevenD99"><font color="#030" face="High Tower Text">Talk</font></a> | <a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/StevenD99" title="Special:Contributions/StevenD99"><font color="#030" face="High Tower Text">Stalk</font></a></sup> 23:04, 24 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
</ul>
<p>How is this any different than tebowing? <span style="font-size: smaller;" class="autosigned">— Preceding <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Signatures" title="Wikipedia:Signatures">unsigned</a> comment added by <a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/66.229.247.234" title="Special:Contributions/66.229.247.234">66.229.247.234</a> (<a href="/w/index.php?title=User_talk:66.229.247.234&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User talk:66.229.247.234 (page does not exist)">talk</a>) 01:05, 25 August 2013 (UTC)</span></p>
<dl>
<dd>@66.229.247.234: <a href="/wiki/Tebowing" title="Tebowing" class="mw-redirect">tebowing</a> is discussed widely in <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:RS" title="Wikipedia:RS" class="mw-redirect">reliable sources</a>, such as Time, NYT, and has a lasting impact, for example, in recognition as an English word and as a feature in a video game. <a href="/wiki/User:Chris857" title="User:Chris857">Chris857</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Chris857" title="User talk:Chris857">talk</a>) 02:30, 25 August 2013 (UTC)
<dl>
<dd>And with all that, it still doesn't get its own article. <a href="/wiki/User:Ansh666" title="User:Ansh666">Ansh</a><i><a href="/wiki/User_talk:Ansh666" title="User talk:Ansh666">6</a><a href="/wiki/Special:EmailUser/Ansh666" title="Special:EmailUser/Ansh666">6</a><a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/Ansh666" title="Special:Contributions/Ansh666">6</a></i> 02:50, 25 August 2013 (UTC)

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Herbert_Wetterauer"><a href="/wiki/Herbert_Wetterauer" title="Herbert Wetterauer">Herbert Wetterauer</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Herbert_Wetterauer&amp;action=edit&amp;section=T-1" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Herbert Wetterauer">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Herbert_Wetterauer&amp;veaction=edit&amp;section=T-1" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Herbert Wetterauer" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl>
<dd><span id="Herbert_Wetterauer"></span><span class="plainlinks nourlexpansion lx"><a href="/wiki/Herbert_Wetterauer" title="Herbert Wetterauer">Herbert Wetterauer</a> <tt>(</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Herbert_Wetterauer&amp;action=edit">edit</a><tt>|</tt><a href="/wiki/Talk:Herbert_Wetterauer" title="Talk:Herbert Wetterauer">talk</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Herbert_Wetterauer&amp;action=history">history</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Herbert_Wetterauer&amp;action=protect">protect</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Whatlinkshere/Herbert_Wetterauer&amp;limit=999">links</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Herbert_Wetterauer&amp;action=watch">watch</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;page=Herbert+Wetterauer">logs</a><tt>)</tt></span> – (<a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Herbert_Wetterauer" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Herbert Wetterauer">View AfD</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://toolserver.org/~snottywong/cgi-bin/votecounter.cgi?page=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Herbert_Wetterauer">Stats</a></span>)</dd>
<dd>(<span class="plainlinks" style=""><i>Find sources:</i>&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?as_eq=wikipedia&amp;q=%22Herbert+Wetterauer%22&amp;num=50">"Herbert Wetterauer"</a>&#160;–&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?q=%22Herbert+Wetterauer%22&amp;tbm=nws&amp;tbs=ar:1">news</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?tbs=bks:1&amp;q=%22Herbert+Wetterauer%22">books</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://scholar.google.com/scholar?q=%22Herbert+Wetterauer%22">scholar</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.jstor.org/action/doBasicSearch?Query=%22Herbert+Wetterauer%22&amp;acc=on&amp;wc=on">JSTOR</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://images.google.com/images?safe=off&amp;as_rights=(cc_publicdomain%7ccc_attribute%7ccc_sharealike%7ccc_noncommercial%7ccc_nonderived)&amp;q=%22Herbert+Wetterauer%22">free images</a></span>)</dd>
</dl>
<p>Little or no rationale for notability. Dearth of acceptable sources. Article's creator used this as a launching platform for inserting images by the artist into multiple articles. <a href="/wiki/User:JNW" title="User:JNW">JNW</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:JNW" title="User talk:JNW">talk</a>) 03:53, 21 August 2013 (UTC)</p>
<dl>
<dd><small class="delsort-notice">Note: This debate has been included in the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Deletion_sorting/Germany" title="Wikipedia:WikiProject Deletion sorting/Germany">list of Germany-related deletion discussions</a>. <a href="/wiki/User:Gene93k" title="User:Gene93k">• Gene93k</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Gene93k" title="User talk:Gene93k">talk</a>) 14:06, 21 August 2013 (UTC)</small></dd>
<dd><small class="delsort-notice">Note: This debate has been included in the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Deletion_sorting/Visual_arts" title="Wikipedia:WikiProject Deletion sorting/Visual arts">list of Visual arts-related deletion discussions</a>. <a href="/wiki/User:Gene93k" title="User:Gene93k">• Gene93k</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Gene93k" title="User talk:Gene93k">talk</a>) 14:06, 21 August 2013 (UTC)</small></dd>
<dd><small class="delsort-notice">Note: This debate has been included in the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Deletion_sorting/People" title="Wikipedia:WikiProject Deletion sorting/People">list of People-related deletion discussions</a>. <a href="/wiki/User:Gene93k" title="User:Gene93k">• Gene93k</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Gene93k" title="User talk:Gene93k">talk</a>) 14:06, 21 August 2013 (UTC)</small></dd>
</dl>
<p><b>Keep.</b> I cannot understand <a href="/wiki/User:JNW" title="User:JNW">JNW</a>'s claim about "little or no rationale for notability", because <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:ARTIST" title="Wikipedia:ARTIST" class="mw-redirect">WP:ARTIST</a>/<a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:AUTHOR" title="Wikipedia:AUTHOR" class="mw-redirect">WP:AUTHOR</a> is clearly met: Herbert Wetterauer has published several books and his artwork was featured in a number of exhibitions.--<a href="/wiki/User:FoxyOrange" title="User:FoxyOrange">FoxyOrange</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:FoxyOrange" title="User talk:FoxyOrange">talk</a>) 17:01, 22 August 2013 (UTC)</p>
<ul>
<li><b>Comment</b> I can't see that any of the criteria for <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:ARTIST" title="Wikipedia:ARTIST" class="mw-redirect">WP:ARTIST</a>/<a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:AUTHOR" title="Wikipedia:AUTHOR" class="mw-redirect">WP:AUTHOR</a> are met. There's no indication that <i>The person is regarded as an important figure or is widely cited by peers or successors; The person is known for originating a significant new concept, theory or technique; The person has created, or played a major role in co-creating, a significant or well-known work, or collective body of work, that has been the subject of an independent book or feature-length film, or of multiple independent periodical articles or reviews</i>; or that <i>The person's work (or works) either (a) has become a significant monument, (b) has been a substantial part of a significant exhibition, (c) has won significant critical attention, or (d) is represented within the permanent collections of several notable galleries or museums</i>.</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dd>Perhaps on the last criteria, Art-Collection Westermann, City-Gallery of Rastatt or One-Man-Show at the State Art Museum Baden-Baden offer some possibility, but neither is sourced, and there's little indication that either venue is significant--is either represented by a separate article on Wikipedia? The other galleries appear to be commercial or otherwise have no claim to notability. Similarly, merely publishing books establishes nothing, other than having published books. <a href="/wiki/User:JNW" title="User:JNW">JNW</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:JNW" title="User talk:JNW">talk</a>) 17:27, 22 August 2013 (UTC)</dd>
</dl>

<dl>
<dd><span id="Philip_Nadelman"></span><span class="plainlinks nourlexpansion lx"><a href="/wiki/Philip_Nadelman" title="Philip Nadelman">Philip Nadelman</a> <tt>(</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Philip_Nadelman&amp;action=edit">edit</a><tt>|</tt><a href="/wiki/Talk:Philip_Nadelman" title="Talk:Philip Nadelman">talk</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Philip_Nadelman&amp;action=history">history</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Philip_Nadelman&amp;action=protect">protect</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Whatlinkshere/Philip_Nadelman&amp;limit=999">links</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Philip_Nadelman&amp;action=watch">watch</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;page=Philip+Nadelman">logs</a><tt>)</tt></span> – (<a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Philip_Nadelman" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Philip Nadelman">View AfD</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://toolserver.org/~snottywong/cgi-bin/votecounter.cgi?page=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Philip_Nadelman">Stats</a></span>)</dd>

<p>No significant independent coverage. Is writing one song enought to establish notability? <a href="/wiki/User:Wkharrisjr" title="User:Wkharrisjr">Wkharrisjr</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Wkharrisjr" title="User talk:Wkharrisjr">talk</a>) 19:46, 20 August 2013 (UTC)</p>

<ul>
<li><b>Keep</b> - This is a <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:STUB" title="Wikipedia:STUB" class="mw-redirect">stub</a> which by definition means it is not yet expanded into a full-fledged article. No one said that his "writing one song" establishes his notability per se (although indeed sometimes writing one song does establish notability). Nadleman is primarily an artist whose work has been shown in various venues, so it would seem that outside evaluators have deemed his work worthy of exhibit. I think if we want to improve the encyclopedia we should not be wasting energy discussing and eliminating stubs but rather work on expanding them. <strong><a href="/wiki/User:Tvoz" title="User:Tvoz">Tvoz</a></strong>/<small><a href="/wiki/User_talk:Tvoz" title="User talk:Tvoz">talk</a></small> 02:43, 21 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dd>True, but how long does a stub exist before it becomes obvious that it will not be expanded? This particular stub dates back to 2007.<a href="/wiki/User:Wkharrisjr" title="User:Wkharrisjr">Wkharrisjr</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Wkharrisjr" title="User talk:Wkharrisjr">talk</a>) 15:07, 21 August 2013 (UTC)</dd>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><b>Delete</b>. Simply being a stub isn't a defence to deletion. This article has no references establishing the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:N" title="Wikipedia:N" class="mw-redirect">notability</a> of the subject—the first is a primary source (an autobiography) and the second is a chart listing for a different artist which doesn't mention Nadelman at all. —<a href="/wiki/User:Psychonaut" title="User:Psychonaut">Psychonaut</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Psychonaut" title="User talk:Psychonaut">talk</a>) 17:18, 21 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
</ul>

<ul>
<li><b>Delete</b> Pretty much says he is non-notable. <a href="/wiki/User:Johnbod" title="User:Johnbod">Johnbod</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Johnbod" title="User talk:Johnbod">talk</a>) 17:55, 20 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
<li><b>Weak Keep</b> My first reaction was "get real," and I was all set to delete it. And my first Google News search turned up only other people with similar names. But refining the search I found quite a few items at Google News. I have added several references to the (previously uncited) article; there were others behind paywalls. I think he may be notable enough for an article here. --<a href="/wiki/User:MelanieN" title="User:MelanieN">MelanieN</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:MelanieN" title="User talk:MelanieN">talk</a>) 18:59, 23 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
<li><b>Strong Keep</b> In the world of origami, which most people don't really know much about in the first place, Jeremy Shafer is brilliant. He comes up with new designs about every other week, and figured out how to make <a href="/wiki/Akira_Yoshizawa" title="Akira Yoshizawa">Akira Yoshizawa's</a> self-portrait just by looking at a picture of it (there are no diagrams). He has also published books and diagrams. I agree that this article can be improved, but it <i>certainly</i> should not be deleted. Thanks for any consideration of my input. <a href="/wiki/User:Ensignricky" title="User:Ensignricky">Ensignricky</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Ensignricky" title="User talk:Ensignricky">talk</a>) 21:36, 26 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
<li><b>Keep</b> Jeremy Shafer is the top of his field; just because it is a fairly uncelebrated field doesn't mean it's unimportant or useless. Much like our pages on chess champs such as <a href="/wiki/Garry_Kasparov" title="Garry Kasparov">Garry Kasparov</a>, he's a well-known figure in origami, and has plenty of fans and followers. If that doesn't make him "important" or "enough of a celebrity", then Wikipedia is denying its users the right of knowledge, which is the reason they come here in the first place. This page does require some development, but deletion is the last thing it needs. <a href="/wiki/User:Vulpa" title="User:Vulpa"><b><font color="#FF4500">V</font><font color="#FF8C00">u</font><font color="#FFA500">l</font><font color="#FFD700">p</font><font color="#FFFF00">a</font></b></a> 13:19, 27 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
</ul>

Wikipedia has <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Policies_and_guidelines" title="Wikipedia:Policies and guidelines">policies and guidelines</a> regarding the encyclopedia's content, and <b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Consensus" title="Wikipedia:Consensus">consensus</a></b> (agreement) is gauged based on the merits of the arguments, <i>not</i> by counting votes.

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Functional_Surrealism"><a href="/wiki/Functional_Surrealism" title="Functional Surrealism">Functional Surrealism</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Functional_Surrealism&amp;action=edit&amp;section=T-1" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Functional Surrealism">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Functional_Surrealism&amp;veaction=edit&amp;section=T-1" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Functional Surrealism" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl>
<dd><span id="Functional_Surrealism"></span><span class="plainlinks nourlexpansion lx"><a href="/wiki/Functional_Surrealism" title="Functional Surrealism">Functional Surrealism</a> <tt>(</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Functional_Surrealism&amp;action=edit">edit</a><tt>|</tt><a href="/wiki/Talk:Functional_Surrealism" title="Talk:Functional Surrealism">talk</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Functional_Surrealism&amp;action=history">history</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Functional_Surrealism&amp;action=protect">protect</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Whatlinkshere/Functional_Surrealism&amp;limit=999">links</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Functional_Surrealism&amp;action=watch">watch</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;page=Functional+Surrealism">logs</a><tt>)</tt></span> – (<a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Functional_Surrealism" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Functional Surrealism">View AfD</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://toolserver.org/~snottywong/cgi-bin/votecounter.cgi?page=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Functional_Surrealism">Stats</a></span>)</dd>
<dd>(<span class="plainlinks" style=""><i>Find sources:</i>&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?as_eq=wikipedia&amp;q=%22Functional+Surrealism%22&amp;num=50">"Functional Surrealism"</a>&#160;–&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?q=%22Functional+Surrealism%22&amp;tbm=nws&amp;tbs=ar:1">news</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?tbs=bks:1&amp;q=%22Functional+Surrealism%22">books</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://scholar.google.com/scholar?q=%22Functional+Surrealism%22">scholar</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.jstor.org/action/doBasicSearch?Query=%22Functional+Surrealism%22&amp;acc=on&amp;wc=on">JSTOR</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://images.google.com/images?safe=off&amp;as_rights=(cc_publicdomain%7ccc_attribute%7ccc_sharealike%7ccc_noncommercial%7ccc_nonderived)&amp;q=%22Functional+Surrealism%22">free images</a></span>)</dd>
</dl>
<p>This was deprodded without explanation. The term is a non-notable neologism (coined in 2010 apparently) with no independent sources. The article reads like an essay and is basically original research. What sources that have been added have no connection to the topic (most reference <a href="/wiki/Surrealism" title="Surrealism">surrealism</a>) and essentially serve to point out that this article is original research and there is no use of the term outside the context of the artist who coined it. Fails <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:GNG" title="Wikipedia:GNG" class="mw-redirect">WP:GNG</a>. <a href="/wiki/User:Freshacconci" title="User:Freshacconci"><b><font color="#000000">freshacconci</font></b></a> <a href="/wiki/User_talk:Freshacconci" title="User talk:Freshacconci"><b><font color="#B22222">talk</font> <font color="#2F4F4F">to me</font></b></a> 00:56, 20 August 2013 (UTC)</p>

<li><b>Delete</b> per nom. <a href="/wiki/User:Johnbod" title="User:Johnbod">Johnbod</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Johnbod" title="User talk:Johnbod">talk</a>) 01:22, 20 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
<li><b>Delete</b> The article is a consumer of its references rather than being supported by them: reton, Kaprow and Rosemont all precede the positing of this proposed movement by one or two generations. No evidence that it is notable in itself. <a href="/wiki/User:AllyD" title="User:AllyD">AllyD</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:AllyD" title="User talk:AllyD">talk</a>) 06:13, 20 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
<li><b>Keep</b>The article is about an art movement originated in 2010 and a manifest that the artist, Philip Henderickx and Marie Daelemans published in 2010, the manifest and the art movement refers to sources and terms used in those articles and so have a connection to this article. The sources that have been added have connection to the article as the manifesto reference to terms of surrealism / Fluxus / Happening / other noted articles. The article is not original research, it is an growing art movement in central Europe, several art manifestations happened under this term and so is larger than only the context of the artists mentioned in it. <a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/81.82.215.154" title="Special:Contributions/81.82.215.154">81.82.215.154</a> (<a href="/w/index.php?title=User_talk:81.82.215.154&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User talk:81.82.215.154 (page does not exist)">talk</a>) 12:27, 20 August 2013 (UTC) <small>— <a href="/w/index.php?title=User:81.82.215.154&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User:81.82.215.154 (page does not exist)">81.82.215.154</a> (<a href="/w/index.php?title=User_talk:81.82.215.154&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User talk:81.82.215.154 (page does not exist)">talk</a> • <a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/81.82.215.154" title="Special:Contributions/81.82.215.154">contribs</a>) has made <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Single-purpose_account" title="Wikipedia:Single-purpose account">few or no other edits</a> outside this topic.</small></li>
<li><b>Keep</b> I understand the concern of freshacconci, have added more references to the article on Functional Surrealism, this article is a reference to an existing art movement and is not an original research. <a href="/w/index.php?title=User:Thosewhogetit&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User:Thosewhogetit (page does not exist)">Thosewhogetit</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Thosewhogetit" title="User talk:Thosewhogetit">talk</a>) 13:38, 20 August 2013 (UTC)<small>— <a href="/w/index.php?title=User:Thosewhogetit&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User:Thosewhogetit (page does not exist)">Thosewhogetit</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Thosewhogetit" title="User talk:Thosewhogetit">talk</a> • <a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/Thosewhogetit" title="Special:Contributions/Thosewhogetit">contribs</a>) has made <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Single-purpose_account" title="Wikipedia:Single-purpose account">few or no other edits</a> outside this topic.</small>
<ul>
<li>There is only one reference that appears to be about the concept. All other references are either about other topics or are closely associated with the artists. References need to be independent of the subject and need to indicate that there is usage of the term beyond the artists who created it. So far, there is no evidence of that. New art movements rarely gain enough traction to be able to be the topic of a Wikipedia article. Wikipedia is not meant to help establish a concept. It needs to be already established. <a href="/wiki/User:Freshacconci" title="User:Freshacconci"><b><font color="#000000">freshacconci</font></b></a> <a href="/wiki/User_talk:Freshacconci" title="User talk:Freshacconci"><b><font color="#B22222">talk</font> <font color="#2F4F4F">to me</font></b></a> 13:58, 20 August 2013 (UTC)
<ul>
<li>I will contact the artists to find more online references, however the mentioned articles in Bibliography are published articles on the matter, will update asap.<a href="/w/index.php?title=User:Thosewhogetit&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User:Thosewhogetit (page does not exist)">Thosewhogetit</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Thosewhogetit" title="User talk:Thosewhogetit">talk</a>) 14:31, 20 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><b>Delete</b> Per above discussion establishing that this is a neologism that is not notable. <a href="/wiki/User:Candleabracadabra" title="User:Candleabracadabra">Candleabracadabra</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Candleabracadabra" title="User talk:Candleabracadabra">talk</a>) 04:09, 21 August 2013 (UTC)</li>

<li><b>Delete</b> as indulgent dross. <a href="/wiki/User:Xxanthippe" title="User:Xxanthippe">Xxanthippe</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Xxanthippe" title="User talk:Xxanthippe">talk</a>) 22:30, 17 August 2013 (UTC).</li>
<li><b>Weak delete</b>. His piece at the Venice Biennale may actually be notable <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.blouinartinfo.com/news/story/32049/chinese-artist-locks-himself-in-a-box-in-venice/">[4]</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.mediabistro.com/unbeige/in-venice-an-artist-thinks-inside-the-box_b7073">[5]</a>. But the article as it stands is in such bad shape that <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:TNT" title="Wikipedia:TNT" class="mw-redirect">WP:TNT</a> may be warranted. —<a href="/wiki/User:David_Eppstein" title="User:David Eppstein">David Eppstein</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:David_Eppstein" title="User talk:David Eppstein">talk</a>) 17:12, 18 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
<li><b>Keep</b>. Need I remind people that neither a conflict of interest nor an article being "indulgent dross" are reasons for deletion? I would agree with <a href="/wiki/User:David_Eppstein" title="User:David Eppstein">David Eppstein</a> that the article may require a complete rewrite to bring it up to standards, but articles in the LA Times, Il Giornale, Express India and Telegraph and possibly some Chinese-language publications establish notability as does the artist's exhibition record. There appear to be a number of other <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:RS" title="Wikipedia:RS" class="mw-redirect">WP:RSs</a> that further help pass both <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:GNG" title="Wikipedia:GNG" class="mw-redirect">WP:GNG</a> and <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:ARTIST" title="Wikipedia:ARTIST" class="mw-redirect">WP:ARTIST</a>. The conflict of interest can be dealt with and the "dross" can be edited out. If the book <i>Personal Structures: Time-Space-Existence</i> can be verified to include substantial material on the artist (I can't find a table of contents or index online), that would also go towards firmly establishing notability but I believe that is already established by the other sources available. <a href="/wiki/User:Freshacconci" title="User:Freshacconci"><b><font color="#000000">freshacconci</font></b></a> <a href="/wiki/User_talk:Freshacconci" title="User talk:Freshacconci"><b><font color="#B22222">talk</font> <font color="#2F4F4F">to me</font></b></a> 15:39, 19 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
<li><b>Keep</b>. Credible sources that establish notability. <a href="/wiki/User:Elfpunk" title="User:Elfpunk">Elfpunk</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Elfpunk" title="User talk:Elfpunk">talk</a>) 22:05, 21 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
</ul>

<li>Comment - Calise - I think you're not understanding what notability means. Having your name mentioned in a list of every Algerian artist when you're an Algerian artist is not a sign of notability. Having an announcement by a radio station that you're going to be on the show, is not a sign of notability. A routine PR release stating he's having an exhibit does not show notability. A biography page written directly by the subject does not show notability. Bottom line, yes there's tons of hits for his name. However the hits are not in articles about the subject, they're all either 1)Routine PR releases, 2)Facebook type pages edited by the subject/his PR team, 3)Blogs - Which are mainly just re-posting the announcements/PR releases, 4)Bio pages written directly by the subject or 5)His name being mentioned along with everyone else that qualifies in a book listing all "Algerian Artists". Yes I took a look at each page you posted, they're all the same missing the same things. <a href="/wiki/User:Caffeyw" title="User:Caffeyw">Caffeyw</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Caffeyw" title="User talk:Caffeyw">talk</a>) 00:16, 25 August 2013 (UTC)</li>

<dl>
<dd>No you didn't. <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:RS" title="Wikipedia:RS" class="mw-redirect">Reliable sources</a> are <i>media coverage</i> (newspapers, books, magazines, etc.) which is <i>independent</i> of the subject himself. Press releases do not count; his own website does not count; the webpages of galleries that have booked shows with him do not count; Wordpress blog entries do not count. And it is not sufficient for his name to merely be <i>mentioned</i> on a page (routine event listings, simple lists of artists, etc.), either. It is <i>not</i> enough to just be able to show sources which demonstrate that he <i>exists</i>; he has to be the <b>primary subject</b> of <b>substantial coverage</b> in <b>reliable sources</b>. So no, I'm sorry, but not even one of those links gets him past <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:GNG" title="Wikipedia:GNG" class="mw-redirect">WP:GNG</a>. (The Radio-Canada link <i>would</i> count if it was to the real interview, but not if it's just to the <i>episode summary</i>.) Show me articles about him in the arts section of <i><a href="/wiki/Le_Devoir" title="Le Devoir">Le Devoir</a></i> or <i><a href="/wiki/Le_Journal_de_Montr%C3%A9al" title="Le Journal de Montréal">Le Journal de Montréal</a></i>, show me a television interview on <a href="/wiki/T%C3%A9l%C3%A9vision_de_Radio-Canada" title="Télévision de Radio-Canada">Radio-Canada</a>'s or <a href="/wiki/TVA_(Canada)" title="TVA (Canada)">TVA</a>'s arts magazine shows, show me he's been on <i><a href="/wiki/Michel_D%C3%A9sautels" title="Michel Désautels">Désautels</a></i> (or dig out the actual <i>Tam-Tam</i> interview and not just the listing), show me feature articles about him in real magazines, and then maybe we'll talk. <a href="/wiki/User:Bearcat" title="User:Bearcat">Bearcat</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Bearcat" title="User talk:Bearcat">talk</a>) 06:37, 25 August 2013 (UTC)</dd>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Writers_and_critics">Writers and critics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:WikiProject_Biography/Arts_and_entertainment&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Writers and critics">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:WikiProject_Biography/Arts_and_entertainment&amp;veaction=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Writers and critics" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div style="border: 2px solid #484898; background: #FFF; padding: 1ex 1ex 1ex 1.5ex; margin: 0px 0px 10px 0px; font-size: 90%">
<div style="border-bottom: 2px dotted #484898; font-size: 110%"><b>Arts and Entertainment Work Group - Writers and critics</b></div>
<p>The Arts and Entertainment Work Group - Writers and critics is a working group of members of the Biography WikiProject dedicated to ensuring quality and coverage of biography articles.<br /></p>
<div style="border-bottom: 2px dotted #484898; margin-top:5px;"><b>Related Projects</b></div>
<p>Since biographies are potentially under the purview of almost all WikiProjects, it is important that we work in tandem with these projects. Also, when seeking collaboration on articles, don't neglect to approach WikiProjects that are part of the geographical region your subject is/was in.</p>
<div style="border-bottom: 2px dotted #484898; margin-top:5px;"><b>Related Portals</b></div>
<p>Increase the exposure of our work group by nominating our articles for their Portal FA and DYKs. Of course, don't forget the main portal, <a href="/wiki/Portal:Arts" title="Portal:Arts">Portal:Arts</a></p>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Portal:Literature" title="Portal:Literature">Portal:Literature</a></li>
</ul>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Authors">Authors</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:WikiProject_Deletion_sorting/Authors&amp;action=edit&amp;section=T-1" title="Wikipedia:WikiProject Deletion sorting/Authors">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:WikiProject_Deletion_sorting/Authors&amp;veaction=edit&amp;section=T-1" title="Wikipedia:WikiProject Deletion sorting/Authors" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Paul_Kimball"><a href="/wiki/Paul_Kimball" title="Paul Kimball">Paul Kimball</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Paul_Kimball&amp;action=edit&amp;section=T-1" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Paul Kimball">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Paul_Kimball&amp;veaction=edit&amp;section=T-1" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Paul Kimball" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<p>Does not meet <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:AUTHOR" title="Wikipedia:AUTHOR" class="mw-redirect">WP:AUTHOR</a> or <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:FILMMAKER" title="Wikipedia:FILMMAKER" class="mw-redirect">WP:FILMMAKER</a>, appears to be an article written by a COI account. <a href="/wiki/User:LuckyLouie" title="User:LuckyLouie">LuckyLouie</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:LuckyLouie" title="User talk:LuckyLouie">talk</a>) 11:54, 27 August 2013 (UTC)</p>
<ul>
<li><b>Delete</b> per nom. Obviously written by the subject themselves or someone connected to them. Reads like a resume and I'd be surprised if there is anything verifiable available. General rule of thumb, if notability cannot be established beyond primary sources, should be deleted. Too many articles end up getting kept these days based on primary sources alone. <a href="/wiki/User:Laval" title="User:Laval">Laval</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Laval" title="User talk:Laval">talk</a>) 14:22, 27 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
</ul>

<dd>(<span class="plainlinks" style=""><i>Find sources:</i>&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?as_eq=wikipedia&amp;q=%22Karolina+Kr%C3%B3l%22&amp;num=50">"Karolina Król"</a>&#160;–&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?q=%22Karolina+Kr%C3%B3l%22&amp;tbm=nws&amp;tbs=ar:1">news</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?tbs=bks:1&amp;q=%22Karolina+Kr%C3%B3l%22">books</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://scholar.google.com/scholar?q=%22Karolina+Kr%C3%B3l%22">scholar</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.jstor.org/action/doBasicSearch?Query=%22Karolina+Kr%C3%B3l%22&amp;acc=on&amp;wc=on">JSTOR</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://images.google.com/images?safe=off&amp;as_rights=(cc_publicdomain%7ccc_attribute%7ccc_sharealike%7ccc_noncommercial%7ccc_nonderived)&amp;q=%22Karolina+Kr%C3%B3l%22">free images</a></span>)</dd>

<p>Blogger, writer and teenager. Published a single book. I am not seeing any mainstream coverage of her, nor of her book. As far as I can tell, outside of a very mild Polish blogosphere&amp;friends buzz few months ago about "Teeneger publishes a book, cool", there is nothing to support <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:N" title="Wikipedia:N" class="mw-redirect">notability</a>. <sub style="border:1px solid #228B22;padding:1px;"><a href="/wiki/User:Piotrus" title="User:Piotrus">Piotr Konieczny aka Prokonsul Piotrus</a>| <a href="/wiki/User_talk:Piotrus" title="User talk:Piotrus"><font style="color:#7CFC00;background:#006400;">reply here</font></a></sub> 07:54, 27 August 2013 (UTC)</p>

<li><b>Comment</b> I don't know how Geer ranks in notability but that list of papers needs to be cut at least in half. It looks like it was cut and pasted from a CV. <a href="/wiki/User:Liz" title="User:Liz"><font face="Rage Italic" size="4" color="#800080"><i><b>L</b></i>iz</font></a> <sup><font face="Times New Roman" color="#006400"><a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/Liz" title="Special:Contributions/Liz"><i><b>Read!</b></i></a> <a href="/wiki/User_talk:Liz" title="User talk:Liz"><i><b>Talk!</b></i></a></font></sup> 20:04, 26 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
<li><b>Delete</b> Here is <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.legacy.com/obituaries/AugustaChronicle/obituary.aspx?n=William-Dudley-Geer&amp;pid=1458056#fbLoggedOut">William Dudley Geer obituary</a> which verifies most of the article's highlights. The article was created by another Geer <a href="/w/index.php?title=User:SamuelTGeer&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User:SamuelTGeer (page does not exist)">User:SamuelTGeer</a> in 2004, who also uploaded <a class="external text" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:Geer,_James_Frederick_Sr..jpg">old</a> <a class="external text" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:Geer,_Mary_Bethany_%28nee_Callaway%29.jpg">pictures</a> of the Geer family, presently unused. I don't believe any of his many titles or positions pass <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:ACADEMIC" title="Wikipedia:ACADEMIC" class="mw-redirect">WP:ACADEMIC</a>, Dean not high enough. Nothing for <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:GNG" title="Wikipedia:GNG" class="mw-redirect">WP:GNG</a> in Google Books. Nothing in Google Scholar. I checked commercial databases for older offline material (JSTOR, Gale, ProQuest etc) and nothing there. -- <a href="/wiki/User:Green_Cardamom" title="User:Green Cardamom">Green Cardamom</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Green_Cardamom" title="User talk:Green Cardamom">talk</a>) 20:52, 26 August 2013 (UTC)</li>

<p>Non-notable writer and actor, fails <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:AUTHOR" title="Wikipedia:AUTHOR" class="mw-redirect">AUTHOR</a>, <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:NACTOR" title="Wikipedia:NACTOR" class="mw-redirect">NACTOR</a> and <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:GNG" title="Wikipedia:GNG" class="mw-redirect">GNG</a>. <a href="/wiki/User:YousufMiah" title="User:YousufMiah">YousufMiah</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:YousufMiah" title="User talk:YousufMiah">talk</a>) 02:15, 26 August 2013 (UTC)</p>
<ul>
<li><b>Keep</b> - article meets criteria for notability. It asserts notability as a counterculture writer of multiple books and is supported by <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:V" title="Wikipedia:V" class="mw-redirect">verifiable</a>, <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:IS" title="Wikipedia:IS" class="mw-redirect">independent</a> references. <a href="/wiki/User:Reddogsix" title="User:Reddogsix"><font color="red">red</font><font color="black"><b>dog</b></font><font color="black"><i>six</i></font></a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Reddogsix#top" title="User talk:Reddogsix">talk</a>) 02:51, 26 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dd>
<ul>
<li>I actually have to argue against many of the sources as far as notability giving goes. IMDb isn't usable to show notability as anyone can edit it. Merchant sources such as Amazon and CD Universe are really discouraged in general for the obvious reasons (the sites' purpose is to sell you things), and many of the other sources are primary. The NIU source is good, albeit maybe slightly trivial in nature, and the Hartford Courant article is also good. All in all, those are probably the only two sources I'd keep, but we definitely need more as far as showing solid notability goes. I don't think (or at least I hope) that sources will be that hard to find, though. <a href="/wiki/User:Tokyogirl79" title="User:Tokyogirl79">Tokyogirl79</a> <a href="/wiki/User_talk:Tokyogirl79" title="User talk:Tokyogirl79"><b><span style="color: #19197;background-color: #FFFFFF;">(｡◕‿◕｡)</span></b></a> 04:24, 26 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
</ul>
</dd>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><b>Keep</b>. Now that I've cleaned out the blatantly unusable sources, I've managed to add in just enough to where it should be a comfortable enough keep. Now what I didn't add were the amount of sources that listed some of his books as various sources and recommended reading. Here are some of them: <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=iWNAcvEI5DsC&amp;pg=PA431&amp;dq=%22Child's+Garden+of+Grass%22+Margolis&amp;hl=en&amp;sa=X&amp;ei=StwaUvXRFJGY9QTfpIGIAg&amp;ved=0CGAQ6AEwCQ#v=onepage&amp;q=%22Child's%20Garden%20of%20Grass%22%20Margolis&amp;f=false">[49]</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=4neuLF3p5ykC&amp;pg=PA77&amp;dq=%22Jack+S.+Margolis%22&amp;hl=en&amp;sa=X&amp;ei=sNgaUp6SDISC8gTXn4DYAg&amp;ved=0CDYQ6AEwAjgK#v=onepage&amp;q=%22Jack%20S.%20Margolis%22&amp;f=false">[50]</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=V9FE6RvH4pEC&amp;pg=PA155&amp;dq=%22Jack+S.+Margolis%22&amp;hl=en&amp;sa=X&amp;ei=sNgaUp6SDISC8gTXn4DYAg&amp;ved=0CDAQ6AEwATgK#v=onepage&amp;q=%22Jack%20S.%20Margolis%22&amp;f=false">[51]</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=c487w9PuJOgC&amp;pg=PT1226&amp;dq=%22Jack+S.+Margolis%22&amp;hl=en&amp;sa=X&amp;ei=sNgaUp6SDISC8gTXn4DYAg&amp;ved=0CDsQ6AEwAzgK#v=onepage&amp;q=%22Jack%20S.%20Margolis%22&amp;f=false">[52]</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=o4_pLqCOyDsC&amp;pg=PA209&amp;dq=%22Child's+Garden+of+Grass%22+Margolis&amp;hl=en&amp;sa=X&amp;ei=2N0aUr2vNYqE9gSuzYCwAw&amp;ved=0CCwQ6AEwADgU#v=onepage&amp;q=%22Child's%20Garden%20of%20Grass%22%20Margolis&amp;f=false">[53]</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=q2Vjm8k5v6cC&amp;pg=PA244&amp;dq=%22Child's+Garden+of+Grass%22+Margolis&amp;hl=en&amp;sa=X&amp;ei=49waUrb8Bo_a8ATMrYGoCA&amp;ved=0CEIQ6AEwBDgK#v=onepage&amp;q=%22Child's%20Garden%20of%20Grass%22%20Margolis&amp;f=false">[54]</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=eVU_4QMn2kAC&amp;pg=PA481&amp;dq=%22Child's+Garden+of+Grass%22+Margolis&amp;hl=en&amp;sa=X&amp;ei=49waUrb8Bo_a8ATMrYGoCA&amp;ved=0CDYQ6AEwAjgK#v=onepage&amp;q=%22Child's%20Garden%20of%20Grass%22%20Margolis&amp;f=false">[55]</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=JvIyVk2IL_sC&amp;pg=PA342&amp;dq=%22Child's+Garden+of+Grass%22+Margolis&amp;hl=en&amp;sa=X&amp;ei=49waUrb8Bo_a8ATMrYGoCA&amp;ved=0CCwQ6AEwADgK#v=onepage&amp;q=%22Child's%20Garden%20of%20Grass%22%20Margolis&amp;f=false">pharmacology textbook</a>). Some of what I've listed are "pop culture" type books, but Margolis is listed in some textbooks as well. I have a feeling that there is probably more out there that isn't on the internet, which isn't entirely surprising given the time period. There's enough to suggest that his work is still considered relatively influential today. He's not Timothy O'Leary, but he's still notable enough. <a href="/wiki/User:Tokyogirl79" title="User:Tokyogirl79">Tokyogirl79</a> <a href="/wiki/User_talk:Tokyogirl79" title="User talk:Tokyogirl79"><b><span style="color: #19197;background-color: #FFFFFF;">(｡◕‿◕｡)</span></b></a> 04:47, 26 August 2013 (UTC)</li>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sam_Hendricks"><a href="/wiki/Sam_Hendricks" title="Sam Hendricks">Sam Hendricks</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Sam_Hendricks&amp;action=edit&amp;section=T-1" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Sam Hendricks">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Sam_Hendricks&amp;veaction=edit&amp;section=T-1" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Sam Hendricks" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl>
<dd><span id="Sam_Hendricks"></span><span class="plainlinks nourlexpansion lx"><a href="/wiki/Sam_Hendricks" title="Sam Hendricks">Sam Hendricks</a> <tt>(</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Sam_Hendricks&amp;action=edit">edit</a><tt>|</tt><a href="/wiki/Talk:Sam_Hendricks" title="Talk:Sam Hendricks">talk</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Sam_Hendricks&amp;action=history">history</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Sam_Hendricks&amp;action=protect">protect</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Whatlinkshere/Sam_Hendricks&amp;limit=999">links</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Sam_Hendricks&amp;action=watch">watch</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;page=Sam+Hendricks">logs</a><tt>)</tt></span> – (<a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Sam_Hendricks" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Sam Hendricks">View AfD</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://toolserver.org/~snottywong/cgi-bin/votecounter.cgi?page=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Sam_Hendricks">Stats</a></span>)</dd>
<dd>(<span class="plainlinks" style=""><i>Find sources:</i>&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?as_eq=wikipedia&amp;q=%22Sam+Hendricks%22&amp;num=50">"Sam Hendricks"</a>&#160;–&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?q=%22Sam+Hendricks%22&amp;tbm=nws&amp;tbs=ar:1">news</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?tbs=bks:1&amp;q=%22Sam+Hendricks%22">books</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://scholar.google.com/scholar?q=%22Sam+Hendricks%22">scholar</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.jstor.org/action/doBasicSearch?Query=%22Sam+Hendricks%22&amp;acc=on&amp;wc=on">JSTOR</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://images.google.com/images?safe=off&amp;as_rights=(cc_publicdomain%7ccc_attribute%7ccc_sharealike%7ccc_noncommercial%7ccc_nonderived)&amp;q=%22Sam+Hendricks%22">free images</a></span>)</dd>
</dl>
<p>I discovered this through <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Fantasy_Football_Guidebook" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Fantasy Football Guidebook">Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Fantasy Football Guidebook</a>. I had begun to clean up the article (<a class="external text" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Sam_Hendricks&amp;oldid=564422296">original version can be seen here</a>) and quickly found out that there just isn't enough reliable sources to show that Hendricks is particularly noteworthy. His article had only one thing that I could even begin to use as a reliable source and that looks to be local coverage since he lives in Nelson County, which is somewhat close to Lynchburg. He seems to have been somewhat prolific, but not to the point where he'd pass as someone who made an extraordinary contribution to the genre of non-fiction books on fantasy football. I can't see where he's considered to be overwhelmingly notable or important within his niche, (to where he'd be cited several times) as there doesn't seem to really be any in-depth articles about him. The only places that cover him are sites that really wouldn't pass as reliable sources per Wikipedia's guidelines. I don't see where RotoNation.com is really usable as a RS since I can't actually locate the site specifically (it redirects to KFFL, which has no articles on him) and many of the other things that were previously used as sources were just basic links to websites- some of which were primary sources. I just don't see where he particularly warrants an article. I have no problem with someone wanting to userfy this and dig for sources over time, but right now I just don't see where he merits an article. <a href="/wiki/User:Tokyogirl79" title="User:Tokyogirl79">Tokyogirl79</a> <a href="/wiki/User_talk:Tokyogirl79" title="User talk:Tokyogirl79"><b><span style="color: #19197;background-color: #FFFFFF;">(｡◕‿◕｡)</span></b></a> 09:04, 25 August 2013 (UTC)</p>
<dl>
<dd><small class="delsort-notice">Note: This debate has been included in the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Deletion_sorting/Authors" title="Wikipedia:WikiProject Deletion sorting/Authors">list of Authors-related deletion discussions</a>. <a href="/wiki/User:Northamerica1000" title="User:Northamerica1000">Northamerica1000</a><sup><a href="/wiki/User_talk:Northamerica1000" title="User talk:Northamerica1000">(talk)</a></sup> 09:51, 25 August 2013 (UTC)</small></dd>
<dd><small class="delsort-notice">Note: This debate has been included in the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Deletion_sorting/Sports" title="Wikipedia:WikiProject Deletion sorting/Sports">list of Sports-related deletion discussions</a>. <a href="/wiki/User:Northamerica1000" title="User:Northamerica1000">Northamerica1000</a><sup><a href="/wiki/User_talk:Northamerica1000" title="User talk:Northamerica1000">(talk)</a></sup> 09:52, 25 August 2013 (UTC)</small></dd>

<dd><span id="Dale_Pendell"></span><span class="plainlinks nourlexpansion lx"><a href="/wiki/Dale_Pendell" title="Dale Pendell">Dale Pendell</a> <tt>(</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Dale_Pendell&amp;action=edit">edit</a><tt>|</tt><a href="/wiki/Talk:Dale_Pendell" title="Talk:Dale Pendell">talk</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Dale_Pendell&amp;action=history">history</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Dale_Pendell&amp;action=protect">protect</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Whatlinkshere/Dale_Pendell&amp;limit=999">links</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Dale_Pendell&amp;action=watch">watch</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;page=Dale+Pendell">logs</a><tt>)</tt></span> – (<a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Dale_Pendell_(2nd_nomination)" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Dale Pendell (2nd nomination)">View AfD</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://toolserver.org/~snottywong/cgi-bin/votecounter.cgi?page=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Dale_Pendell_(2nd_nomination)">Stats</a></span>)</dd>

<p>Non-notable fringe author and poet. Very little impact at Google Books and Google Scholar; an article about his book series was deleted (prod) as non-notable in 2007. Almost no presence at Google News Archive; I found one review of one of his books by the Los Angeles Times. The only reference in the article is a video of a lecture he gave at Burning Man. <a href="/wiki/User:MelanieN" title="User:MelanieN">MelanieN</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:MelanieN" title="User talk:MelanieN">talk</a>) 23:34, 24 August 2013 (UTC)</p>

<li><b>Comment</b> as has been explained to you at some length, despite your refusal to listen, the reason why this has been nominated again is that it was closed imporoperly before - the reason for deletion is the same as the original policy-based reason for deletion. I do not see any reason why I have to repeat myself. <a href="/wiki/User:Barney_the_barney_barney" title="User:Barney the barney barney">Barney the barney barney</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Barney_the_barney_barney" title="User talk:Barney the barney barney">talk</a>) 11:06, 25 August 2013 (UTC)
<ul>
<li>Nope, Dusti's action was acceptable — you don't have to <i>agree</i> with their decision, but they were entirely within their right to make it. Your first nomination consisted of a <i>question</i> as to <i>whether</i> the article met <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:PROF" title="Wikipedia:PROF" class="mw-redirect">WP:PROF</a> or not — you did not advance a reasoned, comprehensive argument that it <i>objectively</i> failed to meet our inclusion rules, but merely asked for other people to <i>investigate</i> whether it did or not. As noted, there are things you can do — take it to <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:N/N" title="Wikipedia:N/N" class="mw-redirect">WP:N/N</a>, for example — if you have <i>questions</i> about an article's notability and want further <i>investigation</i>, but AFD is <i>not</i> the correct process to use until you can provide clear, unambiguous evidence that the article <i>definitely</i> fails to meet one or more of our inclusion rules and should <i>definitely</i> be deleted on those grounds. An AFD discussion <i>without</i> a deletion rationale <i>can</i> be closed at any time by <i>anyone</i>, and your nomination did not include a deletion rationale — and furthermore, the discussion had in fact been open for a full week already without <i>anyone</i> posting <i>either</i> a keep or deletion rationale. I <i>am</i> an administrator, and I might very well have closed it too if I'd seen it before all of this happened. You certainly do have the right to reopen a new discussion as you've done here — but I do have to warn you that if you don't stop criticizing Dusti and start discussing the <i>article</i>, you are running the risk of a temporary editblock for violating <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:CIVIL" title="Wikipedia:CIVIL" class="mw-redirect">WP:CIVIL</a> and <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:NPA" title="Wikipedia:NPA" class="mw-redirect">WP:NPA</a>. <a href="/wiki/User:Bearcat" title="User:Bearcat">Bearcat</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Bearcat" title="User talk:Bearcat">talk</a>) 22:38, 25 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><b>Comment</b>. As with Cullen328's comment earlier, this "keep" comment fails to address the deletion rationale (i.e., whether the subject passes <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:PROF" title="Wikipedia:PROF" class="mw-redirect">WP:PROF</a>), nor does it provide any other policy-based reason for keeping other than the failure to understand the clearly-worded and policy-based rationale for the previous discussion. —<a href="/wiki/User:David_Eppstein" title="User:David Eppstein">David Eppstein</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:David_Eppstein" title="User talk:David Eppstein">talk</a>) 00:29, 26 August 2013 (UTC)</li>

</li>
<li><b>delete, possibly speedy delete as G11</b> The reason given for deletion was specified as it being questionable whether the individual meets WP:PROF, a perfectly good reason for listing an article here. Asking the nominator to specify it in more exact words insteadtead of saying " Can we check whether this meets WP:PROF please" is mere quibbling--the meaning of the deletion reason is perfectly clear. I consider it reasonable for people to bring a questionable article here and ask for opinions; I do this routinely when it looks dubious but is out of my subject. There is two additional very good reasons for deletion, even deletion via speedy: The biographical part of the article is in large part a copy or very close paraphrase of his bio at Moffit Cancer Center <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.moffitt.org/meet-our-team/our-physicians/mokenge-p-malafa-md">here</a>, and it is an entirely promotional article that would need extensive rewriting beyond normal editing. Personally, I do not think the person is notable enough to be worth doing it. And there is another reason to avoid doing it: the author of this article appears to be an entirely promotional editor writing articles about physicians at the Moffit Cancer Center--and I see no reason to myself do properly the work they are (presumably) being paid for and doing improperly. There is a concentrated campaign at WP for articles on robotic surgery and its practitioners, and this is just one part of it. (I suspect it is an attempt to use us as part of a sales competition between the major manufactures of the multi-million dollar machines used in the field)</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dd>First, with respect to notability. The relevant criterion in WP:PROF is the person being a recognized authority is their subject. For scientific fields, this is normally judged on the basis of citations of the individual's papers. The citations for his most cited papers in Google Scholar are 123, 105, 91, in good journals. The h value is 21. This is not spectacular in the field, but it's good. He is not one of the leading workers in the field: a GS search on the subject shows many papers on vitamin E and cancer with citation ranging from 200 to 3000. <s>He has been on the editorial board of some important journals is his subject, though that alone is not notability, as these are large editorial boards of several dozen people.</s> <i>He has not been on the editorial board of a major journal. (corrected, Aug.26)</i> He is an officer in no national professional association, he is an elected fellow of no professional society, his academic positions have been only as Associate Professor</dd>
<dd>Second, about the promotionalism. The article freely uses adjectives of praise: "many papers"; ":most notable". the "Awards" section consists of directory listings, extremely minor awards, and student awards, and within-university awards. There's nothing here which should even be mentioned in a bio article. The professional work section consists of an overextend discussion mixing in his totally unimportant work with his more important work showing no signs of discriminating between the two. The section on surgical work and his work on preventative guidelines talks about activities where he was a "major player" , or had "involvement" or was "one of the first..." . Etc. etc.</dd>
<dd>I am not particularly happy at Barney letting me do all this checking, instead of trying himself, but he did find an article that needs to be removed. I shall be nominating other related articles for deletion. <b><a href="/wiki/User:DGG" title="User:DGG">DGG</a></b> ( <a href="/wiki/User_talk:DGG" title="User talk:DGG">talk</a> ) 16:42, 25 August 2013 (UTC)</dd>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><b>Keep</b> Seems to meet the standards of WP:PROF specifically:
<ul>
<li><b>1. The person's research has made significant impact in their scholarly discipline, broadly construed, as demonstrated by independent reliable sources</b> In this case Malafa appears to have strong Google scholar rankings, author or co-author of a few hundred papers, cited all over the place. It is evident that he has made a significant impact in his scholarly discipline</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dd>That being said, I do think that the page could use some work. However there's a long stretch of road between "needs work" and "delete." <a href="/wiki/User:Simonm223" title="User:Simonm223">Simonm223</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Simonm223" title="User talk:Simonm223">talk</a>) 00:35, 26 August 2013 (UTC)</dd>

<ul>
<li><b>Weak delete</b>. In his specialty, the use of Vitamin E for cancer prevention/amelioration: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://scholar.google.com/scholar?q=%22Vitamin+E%22+cancer">Google scholar</a> found citation counts of 1552, 960, 674, 651, 541, etc. I conclude from this that this is a high-citation area and that his own citation counts, 123, 105, etc (while nothing to sneeze at) are not enough to make a convincing case for <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:PROF#C1" title="Wikipedia:PROF" class="mw-redirect">WP:PROF#C1</a>. What else is there? Chair of a department is clearly not a high enough level administrative position for WP:PROF, and the awards listed in the article are certainly too low-level to count for much. And I also agree with the promotional language and conflict-of-interest concerns raised by DGG. If he were more clearly notable, I'd suggest stubbing it down to something neutral and better-sourced, but in this case because of the borderline notability and COI issues I think <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:TNT" title="Wikipedia:TNT" class="mw-redirect">WP:TNT</a> is a better choice. —<a href="/wiki/User:David_Eppstein" title="User:David Eppstein">David Eppstein</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:David_Eppstein" title="User talk:David Eppstein">talk</a>) 00:40, 26 August 2013 (UTC)
<ul>
<li><b>Comment</b>: While there are many articles and institutions investigating the role of Vitamin E in cancer prevention, each group investigates specific aspects of this problem: rectal cancer, breast cancer, colon cancer, etc. A quick look at the articles which cite the subject's research will show that only <i>he</i> has conducted research on whether α-TOS can prevent <i>melanoma</i>, for example. Also, the fact that the subject's research is routinely cited, even when the article is dealing with a <i>different</i> application of Vitamin E than the subject deals with, demonstrates, in accordance with <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:PROF" title="Wikipedia:PROF" class="mw-redirect">WP:PROF</a>, the subjects' broad attribution as a pioneer in this area of research:
<ul>
<li>"the [subject] has pioneered or developed a significant new concept, technique or idea, made a significant discovery or solved a major problem in their academic discipline." <a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/72.184.149.224" title="Special:Contributions/72.184.149.224">72.184.149.224</a> (<a href="/w/index.php?title=User_talk:72.184.149.224&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User talk:72.184.149.224 (page does not exist)">talk</a>) 15:22, 26 August 2013 (UTC)
<ul>
<li>If you restrict the author's specialization to Vitamin E for melanoma, this will eliminate three of his five top-cited papers. And even in that highly-specialized subtopic, he does not have the most highly-cited paper (that one is by Prasad and Edwards-Prasad). —<a href="/wiki/User:David_Eppstein" title="User:David Eppstein">David Eppstein</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:David_Eppstein" title="User talk:David Eppstein">talk</a>) 00:19, 27 August 2013 (UTC)</li>

<li><b>Comment</b> I have copyedited a bit, correcting typos and errors. I have removed puffery and promotionalism, including two mentions of the brand name of the robotic surgery gear that he now uses. I have trimmed away some unreferenced material. I am not claiming that the article is without flaws, but I've tried to attack its most glaring defects. Two editors I respect, <a href="/wiki/User:DGG" title="User:DGG">DGG</a> and <a href="/wiki/User:David_Eppstein" title="User:David Eppstein">David Eppstein</a> have recommending deleting while conceding that notability may be possible. DGG described the citation count as "good" but "not spectacular". David Eppstein called the citations "nothing to sneeze at" and conceded "borderline notability". Both expressed concern about promotionalism and COI editing, which can be addressed through the normal editing process, and which I have tried to do in recent hours. I concede that I am weak in assessing the notability of academics, since I am a guy with a bachelor's degree not now involved in academia. But I don't think that the TNT essay applies here, since I honestly don't see the article as "hopelessly irreparable". I encourage everyone participating in this debate to make a thoughtful, constructive edit or three to this article, and add it to your watch lists. Thanks. <a href="/wiki/User:Cullen328" title="User:Cullen328"><b><font color="green">Cullen</font></b><sup><font color="purple">328</font></sup></a> <a href="/wiki/User_talk:Cullen328" title="User talk:Cullen328"><font color="blue"><i>Let's discuss it</i></font></a> 04:03, 26 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
