<dl>
<dd>A year ago I would have agreed with you. What I think we need to do here is add the most important academic people, with the priority for the notable ones, not the ones who havePR agents. If this were an isolated article, I would feel differently, but why should either you or I work at helping someone make all the articles for the borderline people at a particular medical institute? Neither notability nor promotionalism is a black/white issue. In the past I'd keep anything where Notability was borderline unless it was total advertising. Now I would remove anything borderline unless there is no taint of promotionalism, and I would personally not bother rewriting a promotional article unless the subject were actually famous. If I can find a way or proposing this as a formal deletion criterion I will. The danger to WP is not in including marginal articles, but rather is including promotionalism. With different standards of notability, we'd be a more or less complete encyclopedia; with respect to advertising, we wouldn't be an encyclopedia at all. But I will say, that if it is kept, I will fix it further, rather than have it totally misrepresent his importance. Incidentally, I mentioned that he is only an associate professor; a less sophisticated editor would have said this--this avoids saying he has any academic rank at a med school at all, because it would have to say what it was. This is sophisticated WP-aware promotional writing, and therefore all the more dangerous. <b><a href="/wiki/User:DGG" title="User:DGG">DGG</a></b> ( <a href="/wiki/User_talk:DGG" title="User talk:DGG">talk</a> ) 04:31, 26 August 2013 (UTC)
<dl>
<dd>If this is "sophisticated" PR writing, then that industry is not capable of fooling people like you. I can see trying to slip in the brand name of the robotic surgery system, but twice? And scrambling up where he was raised? The reason I chose to try to improve the article is that I am a volunteer and it caught my interest. I can work on any article I want to, and I get some strange pleasure occasionally from saving articles I discover at AfD. I would rather work on a biography of a research physician than an article on an internet meme or anime character. As for him being "only" an associate professor, I don't think that is incompatible with notability at all. <a href="/wiki/User:Cullen328" title="User:Cullen328"><b><font color="green">Cullen</font></b><sup><font color="purple">328</font></sup></a> <a href="/wiki/User_talk:Cullen328" title="User talk:Cullen328"><font color="blue"><i>Let's discuss it</i></font></a> 04:45, 26 August 2013 (UTC)
<dl>
<dd>sophisticated <b>=</b> relatively sophisticated. For the usual really crude stuff, watch CSD. As for associate professors, although it's not a bar, very few of them have ever been found notable here, even from the most important research universities. Personally, I'd put the bar for WP:PROF lower, at a level which would generally include associate professors at major research universities on the same principle as we don't require musicians to have multiple hit records, or professional athletes to play at that level for more than one single game. I get greatest pleasure help in helping individuals, next greatest in helping borderline articles. I now get pleasure only in helping the ones not the products of PR. Tell me, if you wanted to add researchers who made a contribution to the relationship between vitamin E and cancer, wouldn't you want to write articles on the ones with the most notable work? And in fact the most notable work is that vitamin E supplementation has a detrimental effect on cancer, &amp; this referred to in the relevant WP articles, although none of the lead researchers there have WP articles. . (not that his work shows otherwise--if you read careful--it's entirely pre-clinical studies on cell lines and mice.) The impression the article gives, however, is very different, and could best be helped by removing the word cancer from the article so it doesn't show up prominently in G searches for the subject, which it currently does. Unfortunately, this is impossible since whatever minor importance he has a surgeon is in treating cancer. So the net effect of keeping this article is to promote an untested theory which is against the weight of all medical evidence, If we do keep this article i will reduce section 4.1 to one sentence in the research paragraph. <b><a href="/wiki/User:DGG" title="User:DGG">DGG</a></b> ( <a href="/wiki/User_talk:DGG" title="User talk:DGG">talk</a> ) 16:59, 26 August 2013 (UTC)
<dl>
<dd>
<dl>
<dd>BTW I made an error above: he is <i>not</i> on the editorial board of any major journal, just the minor journal published by his own research center: he "has provided ad hoc reviews" for major journals--something so utterly routine for any scientist with a PhD even with no faculty position whatsoever, that it doesn't even contribute to significant content, let alone to notability, and is always removed from articles along with the other fluff. <b><a href="/wiki/User:DGG" title="User:DGG">DGG</a></b> ( <a href="/wiki/User_talk:DGG" title="User talk:DGG">talk</a> ) 17:07, 26 August 2013 (UTC)</dd>

<ul>
<li><b>Comment</b> He is a medical researcher and MD. I'm not sure why this was cross-posted to the Academic &amp; Educators list. I'm not sure within the field of medical research whether he is considered notable but I think different standards apply than are used to assess academic notability. <a href="/wiki/User:Liz" title="User:Liz"><font face="Rage Italic" size="4" color="#800080"><i><b>L</b></i>iz</font></a> <sup><font face="Times New Roman" color="#006400"><a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/Liz" title="Special:Contributions/Liz"><i><b>Read!</b></i></a> <a href="/wiki/User_talk:Liz" title="User talk:Liz"><i><b>Talk!</b></i></a></font></sup> 20:12, 26 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
<li><b>Delete</b> Does not pass the admittedly high criteria for <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:ACADEMIC" title="Wikipedia:ACADEMIC" class="mw-redirect">WP:ACADEMIC</a>, and of course not even close to <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:GNG" title="Wikipedia:GNG" class="mw-redirect">WP:GNG</a>. He appears to be a successful but run-of-the-mill surgical oncologist. His citations at <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://scholar.google.com/scholar?hl=en&amp;q=Mokenge+P.+Malafa&amp;btnG=&amp;as_sdt=1%2C5&amp;as_sdtp=">Google Scholar</a> are OK but nothing to indicate he <s>is a thought leader in his field</s> has made significant impact in his scholarly discipline; his positions held are not remarkable; and the awards listed are trivial. --<a href="/wiki/User:MelanieN" title="User:MelanieN">MelanieN</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:MelanieN" title="User talk:MelanieN">talk</a>) 21:30, 26 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
</ul>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Chris_Kendall"><a href="/wiki/Chris_Kendall" title="Chris Kendall">Chris Kendall</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Chris_Kendall&amp;action=edit&amp;section=T-1" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Chris Kendall">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Chris_Kendall&amp;veaction=edit&amp;section=T-1" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Chris Kendall" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl>
<dd><span id="Chris_Kendall"></span><span class="plainlinks nourlexpansion lx"><a href="/wiki/Chris_Kendall" title="Chris Kendall">Chris Kendall</a> <tt>(</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Chris_Kendall&amp;action=edit">edit</a><tt>|</tt><a href="/wiki/Talk:Chris_Kendall" title="Talk:Chris Kendall">talk</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Chris_Kendall&amp;action=history">history</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Chris_Kendall&amp;action=protect">protect</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Whatlinkshere/Chris_Kendall&amp;limit=999">links</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Chris_Kendall&amp;action=watch">watch</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;page=Chris+Kendall">logs</a><tt>)</tt></span> – (<a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Chris_Kendall" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Chris Kendall">View AfD</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://toolserver.org/~snottywong/cgi-bin/votecounter.cgi?page=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Chris_Kendall">Stats</a></span>)</dd>
<dd>(<span class="plainlinks" style=""><i>Find sources:</i>&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?as_eq=wikipedia&amp;q=%22Chris+Kendall%22&amp;num=50">"Chris Kendall"</a>&#160;–&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?q=%22Chris+Kendall%22&amp;tbm=nws&amp;tbs=ar:1">news</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?tbs=bks:1&amp;q=%22Chris+Kendall%22">books</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://scholar.google.com/scholar?q=%22Chris+Kendall%22">scholar</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.jstor.org/action/doBasicSearch?Query=%22Chris+Kendall%22&amp;acc=on&amp;wc=on">JSTOR</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://images.google.com/images?safe=off&amp;as_rights=(cc_publicdomain%7ccc_attribute%7ccc_sharealike%7ccc_noncommercial%7ccc_nonderived)&amp;q=%22Chris+Kendall%22">free images</a></span>)</dd>
</dl>
<p>A user <a class="external text" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Chris_Kendall&amp;diff=568721684&amp;oldid=567817586">proposed deletion</a> of this article for the following reason:</p>
<p><i>Seems to fail <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:N" title="Wikipedia:N" class="mw-redirect">WP:N</a> and <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:ENT" title="Wikipedia:ENT" class="mw-redirect">WP:ENT</a>. References are exclusively YouTube, Twitter and other non-notable sources. A Google News search for <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.google.com/search?hl=en&amp;gl=uk&amp;tbm=nws&amp;authuser=0&amp;q=%22chris+kendall%22&amp;oq=%22chris+kendall%22&amp;gs_l=news-cc.3..43j43i53.549.1662.0.1721.14.6.0.4.0.1.283.858.1j4j1.6.0...0.0...1ac.1.PIiomor79_g#authuser=0&amp;bav=on.2,or.r_qf.&amp;fp=d3adfbf38c9a4b7a&amp;gl=uk&amp;hl=en&amp;q=%22chris+kendall%22+crabstickz&amp;tbm=nws&amp;tbs=ar:1">"chris kendall" crabstickz</a> returns no results.</i></p>
<p>I'm inclined to agree with this rationale, but an IP anon removed the template, so procedural nom. <a href="/wiki/User:A_Thousand_Doors" title="User:A Thousand Doors">A Thousand Doors</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:A_Thousand_Doors" title="User talk:A Thousand Doors">talk</a> | <a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/A_Thousand_Doors" title="Special:Contributions/A Thousand Doors">contribs</a>) 14:48, 23 August 2013 (UTC)</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="P._David_Hornik"><a href="/wiki/P._David_Hornik" title="P. David Hornik">P. David Hornik</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/P._David_Hornik&amp;action=edit&amp;section=T-1" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/P. David Hornik">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/P._David_Hornik&amp;veaction=edit&amp;section=T-1" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/P. David Hornik" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="plainlinks ombox ombox-style" style="" role="presentation">
<tr>
<td class="mbox-image"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Polling_is_not_a_substitute_for_discussion" title="Not a vote"><img alt="Not a vote" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/92/Emblem-WikiVote.svg/50px-Emblem-WikiVote.svg.png" width="50" height="50" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/92/Emblem-WikiVote.svg/75px-Emblem-WikiVote.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/92/Emblem-WikiVote.svg/100px-Emblem-WikiVote.svg.png 2x" /></a></td>
<td class="mbox-text" style="">If you came here because someone asked you to, or you read a message on another website, please note that this is <b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Polling_is_not_a_substitute_for_discussion" title="Wikipedia:Polling is not a substitute for discussion">not a majority vote</a></b>, but instead a <i>discussion</i> among Wikipedia contributors. Wikipedia has <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Policies_and_guidelines" title="Wikipedia:Policies and guidelines">policies and guidelines</a> regarding the encyclopedia's content, and <b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Consensus" title="Wikipedia:Consensus">consensus</a></b> (agreement) is gauged based on the merits of the arguments, <i>not</i> by counting votes.
<p>However, you are invited to participate and your opinion is welcome. Remember to <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Assume_good_faith" title="Wikipedia:Assume good faith">assume good faith</a> on the part of others and to <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Signatures" title="Wikipedia:Signatures">sign your posts</a> on this page by adding ~~~~ at the end.</p>
<small><b>Note:</b> Comments by suspected <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Single-purpose_account" title="Wikipedia:Single-purpose account">single-purpose accounts</a> or <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:CANVAS" title="Wikipedia:CANVAS" class="mw-redirect">canvassed</a> users may be tagged using: <code>{{subst:<a href="/wiki/Template:Spa" title="Template:Spa">spa</a>|<i>username</i>}}</code> or <code>{{subst:<a href="/wiki/Template:Canvassed" title="Template:Canvassed">canvassed</a>|<i>username</i>}}</code></small></td>
</tr>

<p>Non-notable columnist, no sources about him found in a search. Prod removed by editor in first edit ever without comment. <a href="/wiki/User:Thargor_Orlando" title="User:Thargor Orlando">Thargor Orlando</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Thargor_Orlando" title="User talk:Thargor Orlando">talk</a>) 14:24, 23 August 2013 (UTC)</p>
<hr />
<ul>
<li>P. David Hornik is an invaluable columnist, writer, and a researcher. A super reporter. It would be a travesty to delete his page!!!, 04:10, 26 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
<li>Hornik is an important columnist whose work appears constantly on two influential, much-trafficked websites, Frontpage Magazine and PJ Media. He is also the author of an outstanding book on Israel, which, published earlier this year, has won critical acclaim as displayed on its Amazon page. Hornik is an important participant in the discourse on Israel and the Middle East in particular.<a href="/w/index.php?title=User:Ace_edotpr&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User:Ace edotpr (page does not exist)">Ace edotpr</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Ace_edotpr" title="User talk:Ace edotpr">talk</a>) 14:41, 23 August 2013 (UTC) <a href="/w/index.php?title=User:Ace_edotpr&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User:Ace edotpr (page does not exist)">Ace edotpr</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Ace_edotpr" title="User talk:Ace edotpr">talk</a>) 14:38, 23 August 2013 (UTC) Ace edotpr (talk) 14:26, 23 August 2013 (UTC) <small><span class="autosigned">— Preceding <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Signatures" title="Wikipedia:Signatures">unsigned</a> comment added by <a href="/w/index.php?title=User:Ace_edotpr&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User:Ace edotpr (page does not exist)">Ace edotpr</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Ace_edotpr" title="User talk:Ace edotpr">talk</a> • <a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/Ace_edotpr" title="Special:Contributions/Ace edotpr">contribs</a>)</span></small></li>
</ul>
<ul>
<li><b>Comment</b>. He's certainly prolific, and he does get mentioned by other writers with similar views. Search is complicated because most of the hits are for his own work; and because there's another David Hornik who's a Silicon Valley investment banker. I found the following: A recent interview of Hornik in <i><a href="/wiki/The_Jewish_Press" title="The Jewish Press">The Jewish Press</a></i>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.jewishpress.com/indepth/interviews-and-profiles/everybodys-aware-that-israels-power-is-growing-an-interview-with-writer-p-david-hornik/2013/07/24/">[56]</a>. Reviews of his book in <i><a href="/wiki/Algemeiner_Journal" title="Algemeiner Journal">Algemeiner Journal</a></i> <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.algemeiner.com/2013/04/25/choosing-life-in-israel-review/">[57]</a>; <i><a href="/wiki/American_Thinker" title="American Thinker">American Thinker</a></i> <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.americanthinker.com/2013/04/choosing_life_in_israel_a_review.html">[58]</a>; the <i><a href="/wiki/Jewish_Ledger" title="Jewish Ledger">Jewish Ledger</a></i> <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.jewishledger.com/2013/04/book-review-choosing-life-in-israel/">[59]</a>, --<a href="/wiki/User:Arxiloxos" title="User:Arxiloxos">Arxiloxos</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Arxiloxos" title="User talk:Arxiloxos">talk</a>) 15:21, 23 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
</ul>

<li><b>Keep</b> per <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:AUTHOR" title="Wikipedia:AUTHOR" class="mw-redirect">WP:AUTHOR</a> #3 (multiple reviews). -- <a href="/wiki/User:Green_Cardamom" title="User:Green Cardamom">Green Cardamom</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Green_Cardamom" title="User talk:Green Cardamom">talk</a>) 18:40, 24 August 2013 (UTC)</li>

<ul>
<li><b>Comment</b> Of course P. David Hornik should have a Wikipedia entry! He is a significant writer for FrontPage Magazine and for PJ Media (two hugely influential American sites)--and for various other online sites. He writes about facets of Jewish life in Israel and the complex politics of the Arab-Israeli conflict--as well as other subjects such as conservatism, Judaism, and the writing life. A recent review of his book, *Choosing Life in Israel,* appeared at FrontPageMag; an interview with him by Jamie Glazov also appears there. He is a well informed commentator, crucial for anyone wanting to understand Israel's position in world affairs.<a href="/w/index.php?title=User:Janice_fiamengo&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User:Janice fiamengo (page does not exist)">Janice fiamengo</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Janice_fiamengo" title="User talk:Janice fiamengo">talk</a>) 19:45, 24 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
</ul>
<ul>
<li>Hornik is a prolific, skillful writer who should definitely have a Wikipedia entry! Not only are his political analyses of the complex situation in the Middle East powerful and insightful (as also manifested in his outstanding book Choosing Life in Israel), but his versatile writings on numerous other topics such as music, near-death experiences, and Judaism are always engaging and astute.<a href="/w/index.php?title=User:Tkrtgnr&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User:Tkrtgnr (page does not exist)">Tkrtgnr</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Tkrtgnr" title="User talk:Tkrtgnr">talk</a>) 20:36, 25 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
</ul>
<ul>
<li>David Hornik is a superbly well-informed and very articulate practitioner of the higher journalism in Israel. Of course he merits recognition in Wikipedia. Edward Alexander, Professor emeritus, University of Washington, Seattle.<small><span class="autosigned">— Preceding <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Signatures" title="Wikipedia:Signatures">unsigned</a> comment added by <a href="/w/index.php?title=User:Eaengl&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User:Eaengl (page does not exist)">Eaengl</a> (<a href="/w/index.php?title=User_talk:Eaengl&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User talk:Eaengl (page does not exist)">talk</a> • <a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/Eaengl" title="Special:Contributions/Eaengl">contribs</a>) 07:08, 25 August 2013 (UTC)</span></small></li>

<li><b>Weak keep</b>. Distinctly borderline case, but there do appear to be just about enough reviews in apparently reliable sources for notability. <a href="/wiki/User:PWilkinson" title="User:PWilkinson">PWilkinson</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:PWilkinson" title="User talk:PWilkinson">talk</a>) 23:43, 25 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
</ul>
<ul>
<li>David Hornik definitely should remain on Wikipedia. He is one of the most articulate spokespersons for a significant point of view on Israel's conflict with the Arabs, not largely heard and coming directly from Israel. His articles are cogent and well researched. He is a prolific writer for on line sites like Frontpage and Pajamas Media and covers a range of issues. He is not only notable but is going to become even more so now that he has begin to write books as well. <a href="/w/index.php?title=User:Gidmeister&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User:Gidmeister (page does not exist)">Gidmeister</a> (<a href="/w/index.php?title=User_talk:Gidmeister&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User talk:Gidmeister (page does not exist)">talk</a>) 12:20, 26 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
</ul>
<ul>
<li>David Hornik is a "boots-on-the-ground," articulate and HONEST voice from Israel. One may disagree with his opinion, but it is disingenuous to argue with the facts he presents. Should he be removed it would be a disservice to the truth...and isn't that what Wikipedia is SUPPOSED to be all about?<a href="/w/index.php?title=User:Newmediajournal&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User:Newmediajournal (page does not exist)">Newmediajournal</a> (<a href="/w/index.php?title=User_talk:Newmediajournal&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User talk:Newmediajournal (page does not exist)">talk</a>) 12:44, 26 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
</ul>
<ul>
<li>David Hornik has a long and distinguished record of commentary on major websites. Disagree or not with his views, he has an enviable record of accurate and pertinent analysis. It would be a disservice to those seeking knowledge to delete his Wikipedia entry. One of the strengths of Wikipedia is the breadth of information it provides on account of the enormous number of entries available. Deletion of his entry would serve no useful public purpose.<a href="/w/index.php?title=User:The_Sirdar&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User:The Sirdar (page does not exist)">TheSirdar</a> (<a href="/w/index.php?title=TheSirdar&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="TheSirdar (page does not exist)">TheSirdar</a>) (<a href="/w/index.php?title=TheSirdar&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="TheSirdar (page does not exist)">TheSirdar</a>) <small><span class="autosigned">— Preceding <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Signatures" title="Wikipedia:Signatures">unsigned</a> comment added by <a href="/w/index.php?title=User:TheSirdar&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User:TheSirdar (page does not exist)">TheSirdar</a> (<a href="/w/index.php?title=User_talk:TheSirdar&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User talk:TheSirdar (page does not exist)">talk</a> • <a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/TheSirdar" title="Special:Contributions/TheSirdar">contribs</a>) 13:19, 26 August 2013 (UTC)</span></small></li>
</ul>
<p>Hornik is sufficiently prolific on frequently-visited sites for there to be substantial interest on the part of numerous readers in obtaining information about him on Wikipedia. The entry should not be deleted. <small><span class="autosigned">— Preceding <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Signatures" title="Wikipedia:Signatures">unsigned</a> comment added by <a href="/w/index.php?title=User:Ronald_Shafran&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User:Ronald Shafran (page does not exist)">Ronald Shafran</a> (<a href="/w/index.php?title=User_talk:Ronald_Shafran&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User talk:Ronald Shafran (page does not exist)">talk</a> • <a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/Ronald_Shafran" title="Special:Contributions/Ronald Shafran">contribs</a>) 15:10, 26 August 2013 (UTC)</span></small></p>
<ul>
<li>It is incomprehensible that deletion of David Hornik's page was even considered. He is one of the most respected Israeli journalists whose columns are reprinted and circulated throughout the internet. They bring a unique perspective to discussion of the Middle East, because he has lived both in America and Israel.Furthermore, his book "Chossing Life In Israel" and the excellent columns on Judaism, history and religion are outstanding.rsk17:03, 26 August 2013 (UTC)17:03, 26 August 2013 (UTC)17:03, 26 August 2013 (UTC)~ <small><span class="autosigned">— Preceding <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Signatures" title="Wikipedia:Signatures">unsigned</a> comment added by <a href="/w/index.php?title=User:Dubceck&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User:Dubceck (page does not exist)">Dubceck</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Dubceck" title="User talk:Dubceck">talk</a> • <a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/Dubceck" title="Special:Contributions/Dubceck">contribs</a>)</span></small></li>
</ul>
<p>Hornik's book is also reviewed here <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://frontpagemag.com/2013/janice-fiamengo/choosing-life-in-israel/">[60]</a> and he's interviewed about the book here <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://frontpagemag.com/2013/jamie-glazov/choosing-life-in-israel-2/">[61]</a>.<a href="/w/index.php?title=User:Ace_edotpr&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User:Ace edotpr (page does not exist)">Ace edotpr</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Ace_edotpr" title="User talk:Ace edotpr">talk</a>) 17:39, 26 August 2013 (UTC, and the book is also featured here <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://daledamos.blogspot.co.il/2013/03/p-david-horniks-first-book-choosing.html">[62]</a>.<a href="/w/index.php?title=User:Ace_edotpr&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User:Ace edotpr (page does not exist)">Ace edotpr</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Ace_edotpr" title="User talk:Ace edotpr">talk</a>) 06:56, 27 August 2013 (UTC)</p>

<li><b>Weak keep</b>. Per above keeps. At the same time, I am troubled by the number of editors with very few edits to their name who have somehow appeared here. That suggests sockpuppetry. See <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:SOCK" title="Wikipedia:SOCK" class="mw-redirect">WP:SOCK</a>. And if it continues, I recommend an investigation, and that any editors found to be socking be blocked. <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Erin_Hart"><a href="/wiki/Erin_Hart" title="Erin Hart">Erin Hart</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Erin_Hart&amp;action=edit&amp;section=T-1" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Erin Hart">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Erin_Hart&amp;veaction=edit&amp;section=T-1" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Erin Hart" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl>
<dd><span id="Erin_Hart"></span><span class="plainlinks nourlexpansion lx"><a href="/wiki/Erin_Hart" title="Erin Hart">Erin Hart</a> <tt>(</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Erin_Hart&amp;action=edit">edit</a><tt>|</tt><a href="/wiki/Talk:Erin_Hart" title="Talk:Erin Hart">talk</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Erin_Hart&amp;action=history">history</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Erin_Hart&amp;action=protect">protect</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Whatlinkshere/Erin_Hart&amp;limit=999">links</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Erin_Hart&amp;action=watch">watch</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;page=Erin+Hart">logs</a><tt>)</tt></span> – (<a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Erin_Hart" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Erin Hart">View AfD</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://toolserver.org/~snottywong/cgi-bin/votecounter.cgi?page=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Erin_Hart">Stats</a></span>)</dd>

<p>Non-<a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:AUTHOR" title="Wikipedia:AUTHOR" class="mw-redirect">notable</a> author. Claims of actual awards have not been verified, and being short-listed for various awards doesn't quite make the mark for <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:AUTHOR" title="Wikipedia:AUTHOR" class="mw-redirect">WP:AUTHOR</a>. No indications of any significant coverage other than the "local interest" piece that is provided as the sole reference for this <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:AUTO" title="Wikipedia:AUTO" class="mw-redirect">autobiography</a>. <a href="/wiki/User:WikiDan61" title="User:WikiDan61"><font color="green">WikiDan61</font></a><sup><a href="/wiki/User_talk:WikiDan61" title="User talk:WikiDan61">ChatMe!</a></sup><sub><a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/WikiDan61" title="Special:Contributions/WikiDan61">ReadMe!!</a></sub> 17:44, 22 August 2013 (UTC)</p>
<ul>
<li><b>Comment</b> Article has been revised to show verification of awards. Still not clear that the awards won (<i>Romantic Times</i> Reviewers' Choice or Friends of American Writers Award) amount to "significant critical attention". I'll defer to others more knowledgeable of the book trade. <a href="/wiki/User:WikiDan61" title="User:WikiDan61"><font color="green">WikiDan61</font></a><sup><a href="/wiki/User_talk:WikiDan61" title="User talk:WikiDan61">ChatMe!</a></sup><sub><a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/WikiDan61" title="Special:Contributions/WikiDan61">ReadMe!!</a></sub> 18:21, 22 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
</ul>

<ul>
<li><b>Weak keep</b> though I can't spot any online reviews of her (minor) award winning 2003 book, <i>Haunted Ground</i> , there are several for her most recent 2013 book <i>The Book of Killowen</i> <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.lavendermagazine.com/our-affairs/books/">[63]</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.startribune.com/entertainment/books/194378411.html">[64]</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.nyjournalofbooks.com/review/book-killowen">[65]</a>. This suggests to me she will at least scrape over the notability threshold of <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:AUTHOR" title="Wikipedia:AUTHOR" class="mw-redirect">WP:AUTHOR</a> (and that there are likely to be other offline(?) coverage of her earlier works). <a href="/wiki/User:Sionk" title="User:Sionk">Sionk</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Sionk" title="User talk:Sionk">talk</a>) 23:49, 22 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
<li><b>Keep</b> per <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:AUTHOR" title="Wikipedia:AUTHOR" class="mw-redirect">WP:AUTHOR</a> #3, multiple reviews. Her book <i>Haunted Ground</i> was reviewed in: New York Times, Publisher's Weekly, Kirkus, Booklist, Book-of-the-month Club, and <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.erinhart.com/haunted-ground.php">many more</a>. <i>Lake of Sorrows</i> was reviewed in New York Times, Publisher's Weekly, Kirkus, Booklist and <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.erinhart.com/lake-of-sorrows.php">many more</a>. -- <a href="/wiki/User:Green_Cardamom" title="User:Green Cardamom">Green Cardamom</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Green_Cardamom" title="User talk:Green Cardamom">talk</a>) 16:48, 23 August 2013 (UTC)</li>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Mir_Najumuddin_Saqib"><a href="/wiki/Mir_Najumuddin_Saqib" title="Mir Najumuddin Saqib">Mir Najumuddin Saqib</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Mir_Najumuddin_Saqib&amp;action=edit&amp;section=T-1" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Mir Najumuddin Saqib">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Mir_Najumuddin_Saqib&amp;veaction=edit&amp;section=T-1" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Mir Najumuddin Saqib" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl>
<dd><span id="Mir_Najumuddin_Saqib"></span><span class="plainlinks nourlexpansion lx"><a href="/wiki/Mir_Najumuddin_Saqib" title="Mir Najumuddin Saqib">Mir Najumuddin Saqib</a> <tt>(</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Mir_Najumuddin_Saqib&amp;action=edit">edit</a><tt>|</tt><a href="/wiki/Talk:Mir_Najumuddin_Saqib" title="Talk:Mir Najumuddin Saqib">talk</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Mir_Najumuddin_Saqib&amp;action=history">history</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Mir_Najumuddin_Saqib&amp;action=protect">protect</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Whatlinkshere/Mir_Najumuddin_Saqib&amp;limit=999">links</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Mir_Najumuddin_Saqib&amp;action=watch">watch</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;page=Mir+Najumuddin+Saqib">logs</a><tt>)</tt></span> – (<a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Mir_Najumuddin_Saqib" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Mir Najumuddin Saqib">View AfD</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://toolserver.org/~snottywong/cgi-bin/votecounter.cgi?page=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Mir_Najumuddin_Saqib">Stats</a></span>)</dd>
<dd>(<span class="plainlinks" style=""><i>Find sources:</i>&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?as_eq=wikipedia&amp;q=%22Mir+Najumuddin+Saqib%22&amp;num=50">"Mir Najumuddin Saqib"</a>&#160;–&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?q=%22Mir+Najumuddin+Saqib%22&amp;tbm=nws&amp;tbs=ar:1">news</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?tbs=bks:1&amp;q=%22Mir+Najumuddin+Saqib%22">books</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://scholar.google.com/scholar?q=%22Mir+Najumuddin+Saqib%22">scholar</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.jstor.org/action/doBasicSearch?Query=%22Mir+Najumuddin+Saqib%22&amp;acc=on&amp;wc=on">JSTOR</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://images.google.com/images?safe=off&amp;as_rights=(cc_publicdomain%7ccc_attribute%7ccc_sharealike%7ccc_noncommercial%7ccc_nonderived)&amp;q=%22Mir+Najumuddin+Saqib%22">free images</a></span>)</dd>
</dl>
<p>Probable hoax? Or maybe transliteration mangling? The two works claimed to have been written are not mentioned anywhere else on the web according to google. I'm not seeing any matches in <a rel="nofollow" class="external free" href="http://viaf.org/">http://viaf.org/</a> or other searches. I'm happy to withdraw the PROD if someone identifies this person in <a rel="nofollow" class="external free" href="http://viaf.org/">http://viaf.org/</a>; comes up with an ISBN of a book by them; or similar. PROD removed with the addition of <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://nyfpk.org/Islam%20in%20Baltistan.php">this link</a> which includes only single passing mention. <a href="/wiki/User:Stuartyeates" title="User:Stuartyeates">Stuartyeates</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Stuartyeates" title="User talk:Stuartyeates">talk</a>) 08:51, 21 August 2013 (UTC)</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sharmi_Albrechtsen"><a href="/wiki/Sharmi_Albrechtsen" title="Sharmi Albrechtsen">Sharmi Albrechtsen</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Sharmi_Albrechtsen&amp;action=edit&amp;section=T-1" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Sharmi Albrechtsen">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Sharmi_Albrechtsen&amp;veaction=edit&amp;section=T-1" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Sharmi Albrechtsen" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="plainlinks ombox ombox-style" style="" role="presentation">
<tr>
<td class="mbox-image"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Polling_is_not_a_substitute_for_discussion" title="Not a vote"><img alt="Not a vote" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/92/Emblem-WikiVote.svg/50px-Emblem-WikiVote.svg.png" width="50" height="50" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/92/Emblem-WikiVote.svg/75px-Emblem-WikiVote.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/92/Emblem-WikiVote.svg/100px-Emblem-WikiVote.svg.png 2x" /></a></td>
<td class="mbox-text" style="">If you came here because someone asked you to, or you read a message on another website, please note that this is <b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Polling_is_not_a_substitute_for_discussion" title="Wikipedia:Polling is not a substitute for discussion">not a majority vote</a></b>, but instead a <i>discussion</i> among Wikipedia contributors. Wikipedia has <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Policies_and_guidelines" title="Wikipedia:Policies and guidelines">policies and guidelines</a> regarding the encyclopedia's content, and <b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Consensus" title="Wikipedia:Consensus">consensus</a></b> (agreement) is gauged based on the merits of the arguments, <i>not</i> by counting votes.
<p>However, you are invited to participate and your opinion is welcome. Remember to <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Assume_good_faith" title="Wikipedia:Assume good faith">assume good faith</a> on the part of others and to <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Signatures" title="Wikipedia:Signatures">sign your posts</a> on this page by adding ~~~~ at the end.</p>
<small><b>Note:</b> Comments by suspected <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Single-purpose_account" title="Wikipedia:Single-purpose account">single-purpose accounts</a> or <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:CANVAS" title="Wikipedia:CANVAS" class="mw-redirect">canvassed</a> users may be tagged using: <code>{{subst:<a href="/wiki/Template:Spa" title="Template:Spa">spa</a>|<i>username</i>}}</code> or <code>{{subst:<a href="/wiki/Template:Canvassed" title="Template:Canvassed">canvassed</a>|<i>username</i>}}</code></small></td>
</tr>

<dl>
<dd><span id="Sharmi_Albrechtsen"></span><span class="plainlinks nourlexpansion lx"><a href="/wiki/Sharmi_Albrechtsen" title="Sharmi Albrechtsen">Sharmi Albrechtsen</a> <tt>(</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Sharmi_Albrechtsen&amp;action=edit">edit</a><tt>|</tt><a href="/wiki/Talk:Sharmi_Albrechtsen" title="Talk:Sharmi Albrechtsen">talk</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Sharmi_Albrechtsen&amp;action=history">history</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Sharmi_Albrechtsen&amp;action=protect">protect</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Whatlinkshere/Sharmi_Albrechtsen&amp;limit=999">links</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Sharmi_Albrechtsen&amp;action=watch">watch</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;page=Sharmi+Albrechtsen">logs</a><tt>)</tt></span> – (<a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Sharmi_Albrechtsen" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Sharmi Albrechtsen">View AfD</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://toolserver.org/~snottywong/cgi-bin/votecounter.cgi?page=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Sharmi_Albrechtsen">Stats</a></span>)</dd>
<dd>(<span class="plainlinks" style=""><i>Find sources:</i>&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?as_eq=wikipedia&amp;q=%22Sharmi+Albrechtsen%22&amp;num=50">"Sharmi Albrechtsen"</a>&#160;–&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?q=%22Sharmi+Albrechtsen%22&amp;tbm=nws&amp;tbs=ar:1">news</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?tbs=bks:1&amp;q=%22Sharmi+Albrechtsen%22">books</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://scholar.google.com/scholar?q=%22Sharmi+Albrechtsen%22">scholar</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.jstor.org/action/doBasicSearch?Query=%22Sharmi+Albrechtsen%22&amp;acc=on&amp;wc=on">JSTOR</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://images.google.com/images?safe=off&amp;as_rights=(cc_publicdomain%7ccc_attribute%7ccc_sharealike%7ccc_noncommercial%7ccc_nonderived)&amp;q=%22Sharmi+Albrechtsen%22">free images</a></span>)</dd>
</dl>
<p>Purely promotional biography about a journalist and a book she's written, with nothing to indicate the notability of the subject. The article in Time Newsfeed has nothing to do with Sharmi Albrechtsen, the article in The Copenhagen Post is about someone else and only mentions Sharmi Albrechtsen briefly and the links to Oprah do not in any way make Sharmi Albrechtsen notable. The impression I get when reading the article is that the subject of it wanted an article about herself on Wikipedia and had someone upload it for her. With one of the reasons for that being that the style of this article is much more polished and grammatically correct than other contributions from the creator of the article (such as this edit summary from <a href="/wiki/Zebra_Finch" title="Zebra Finch">Zebra Finch</a>: <i>I have been bred many times of zebra finch, normally its can give good breed from 6 months of their age</i>), a difference in style and language skills that makes me doubt that the creator wrote it... <a href="/wiki/User:Thomas.W" title="User:Thomas.W"><font face="Comic Sans MS" color="#164D0B"><b>Thomas.W</b></font></a> <a href="/wiki/User_talk:Thomas.W" title="User talk:Thomas.W"><font face="Comic Sans MS" color="#164D0B"><sup><small><b>talk to me</b></small></sup></font></a> 15:26, 20 August 2013 (UTC)</p>

<li><b>Comment</b> Sharmi has an entire page dedicated to all the coverage she has received: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://happydenmark.webs.com/media.htm">Sharmi in the Media</a>. This should be enough for her to be considered notable. <a href="/wiki/User:Mimalman_freeway" title="User:Mimalman freeway">Mimalman freeway</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Mimalman_freeway" title="User talk:Mimalman freeway">talk</a>) 18:59, 20 August 2013 (UTC) <small>— <a href="/wiki/User:Mimalman_freeway" title="User:Mimalman freeway">Mimalman freeway</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Mimalman_freeway" title="User talk:Mimalman freeway">talk</a> • <a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/Mimalman_freeway" title="Special:Contributions/Mimalman freeway">contribs</a>) has made <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Single-purpose_account" title="Wikipedia:Single-purpose account">few or no other edits</a> outside this topic.</small></li>
<li><b>Keep</b> For a blogger and self-published author (Lulu) she has unusual level of international coverage for her book/blog on Danes and happiness, on Oprah's Life Class<a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=L28l3bnIYks">[68]</a>, BBC<a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=P21OMHizaRU">[69]</a>, German television network <a href="/wiki/ARTE" title="ARTE" class="mw-redirect">ARTE</a><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=XCOr87k9vfg">[70]</a>, South Korea's <a href="/wiki/OhMyNews" title="OhMyNews" class="mw-redirect">OhMyNews</a><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.ohmynews.com/NWS_Web/View/at_pg.aspx?CNTN_CD=A0001876844">[71]</a>, <i><a href="/wiki/House_Hunters_International" title="House Hunters International" class="mw-redirect">House Hunters International</a></i> (HGTV)<a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=gY-JQWPJr8s">[72]</a>, Danish lifestyle magazine Mad&amp;Bolig<a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://happydenmark.webs.com/SharmiInMadAndBolig.pdf">[73]</a>. I can't find any book reviews and none of the pieces are really <i>about</i> Sharmi, except <a href="/wiki/OhMyNews" title="OhMyNews" class="mw-redirect">OhMyNews</a>. So there are good and bad here, but I am willing to give her a chance, based on GNG multiple reliable sources. If in 5 or 10 years nothing hew has happened it would be easier delete but don't see the rush to delete yet. -- <a href="/wiki/User:Green_Cardamom" title="User:Green Cardamom">Green Cardamom</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Green_Cardamom" title="User talk:Green Cardamom">talk</a>) 19:56, 20 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
</ul>

<ul>
<li>I have no idea what list you're talking about. As for following you around (I assume you are referring to the fact that I edited the <a href="/wiki/Alice_Crimmins" title="Alice Crimmins">Alice Crimmins</a> article, where your additions have now been removed by multiple editors), it is quite normal to check the contributions of a user who displays some level of <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:COMPETENCE" title="Wikipedia:COMPETENCE" class="mw-redirect">incompetence</a>. As for Bremner, who is the subject of this discussion, it seems to me that you have no idea what "self-published" means. To have publishers like Wiley and Penguin agree to publish your book, you need to do a lot more than just write the book: you will have to go through an extensive review process and having them accept your book proposal is a major accomplishment for an academic. It's nothing like sending your manuscript to one of those vanity publishers and paying them to publish your book for you. And although I'm an old fart who thoroughly dislikes ebooks, I don't see what's wrong with having Kindle versions of a book. And where do you get the "ten copies sold" information from? I don't think that Wiley or Penguin have ever published a book that did not at least sell several hundred copies. As you say indeed: Please! --<a href="/wiki/User:Randykitty" title="User:Randykitty">Randykitty</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Randykitty" title="User talk:Randykitty">talk</a>) 11:20, 23 August 2013 (UTC)</li>

<li><b>Speedy keep</b>. Being an autobio is not a reason for deletion, at most a reason to rewrite an article in a neutral way, if necessary. Given Bremner's stature, the article is remarkably neutral. Let me just give some citation statistics from <a href="/wiki/Web_of_Science" title="Web of Science">Web of Science</a>: 238 publications listed, cited 14885 times, with an <a href="/wiki/H-index" title="H-index">h-index</a> of 65. Top 5 citation counts: 1290, 791, 731, 556, and 350. Just one of those is normally enough here for a "keep" decision. Article certainly needs cleanup and expansion, but Bremner passes <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:ACADEMIC" title="Wikipedia:ACADEMIC" class="mw-redirect">WP:ACADEMIC</a> without any possible doubt. As a note to the nom, please read <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:BEFORE" title="Wikipedia:BEFORE" class="mw-redirect">WP:BEFORE</a> and research nominations better before bringing them to AfD. Thanks. --<a href="/wiki/User:Randykitty" title="User:Randykitty">Randykitty</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Randykitty" title="User talk:Randykitty">talk</a>) 12:21, 20 August 2013 (UTC)</li>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Dashgyn_Gulmammadov"><a href="/wiki/Dashgyn_Gulmammadov" title="Dashgyn Gulmammadov">Dashgyn Gulmammadov</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Dashgyn_Gulmammadov&amp;action=edit&amp;section=T-1" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Dashgyn Gulmammadov">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Dashgyn_Gulmammadov&amp;veaction=edit&amp;section=T-1" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Dashgyn Gulmammadov" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl>
<dd><span id="Dashgyn_Gulmammadov"></span><span class="plainlinks nourlexpansion lx"><a href="/wiki/Dashgyn_Gulmammadov" title="Dashgyn Gulmammadov">Dashgyn Gulmammadov</a> <tt>(</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Dashgyn_Gulmammadov&amp;action=edit">edit</a><tt>|</tt><a href="/wiki/Talk:Dashgyn_Gulmammadov" title="Talk:Dashgyn Gulmammadov">talk</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Dashgyn_Gulmammadov&amp;action=history">history</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Dashgyn_Gulmammadov&amp;action=protect">protect</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Whatlinkshere/Dashgyn_Gulmammadov&amp;limit=999">links</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Dashgyn_Gulmammadov&amp;action=watch">watch</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;page=Dashgyn+Gulmammadov">logs</a><tt>)</tt></span> – (<a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Dashgyn_Gulmammadov" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Dashgyn Gulmammadov">View AfD</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://toolserver.org/~snottywong/cgi-bin/votecounter.cgi?page=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Dashgyn_Gulmammadov">Stats</a></span>)</dd>
<dd>(<span class="plainlinks" style=""><i>Find sources:</i>&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?as_eq=wikipedia&amp;q=%22Dashgyn+Gulmammadov%22&amp;num=50">"Dashgyn Gulmammadov"</a>&#160;–&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?q=%22Dashgyn+Gulmammadov%22&amp;tbm=nws&amp;tbs=ar:1">news</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?tbs=bks:1&amp;q=%22Dashgyn+Gulmammadov%22">books</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://scholar.google.com/scholar?q=%22Dashgyn+Gulmammadov%22">scholar</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.jstor.org/action/doBasicSearch?Query=%22Dashgyn+Gulmammadov%22&amp;acc=on&amp;wc=on">JSTOR</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://images.google.com/images?safe=off&amp;as_rights=(cc_publicdomain%7ccc_attribute%7ccc_sharealike%7ccc_noncommercial%7ccc_nonderived)&amp;q=%22Dashgyn+Gulmammadov%22">free images</a></span>)</dd>
</dl>
<p>The article does not seem fit for Wikipedia for the following reasons:</p>
<ol>
<li>The person whom the article is dedicated to overall does not appear to be very notable.</li>
<li>With the exception of the lead, the article is not sourced at all. However, it makes pretty bold statements with regard to this person's political activity, which may very well be exaggerated, like claiming him to be a 'democracy activist', which a sample check revealed not to be supported by any reliable sources.</li>
<li>The fact that the article has mainly been edited by <a href="/w/index.php?title=User:ARSLANER&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User:ARSLANER (page does not exist)">one user</a> who has not contributed to any other articles on Wikipedia since his/her registration, and also the fact that articles about this person were created en masse in other languages around the same time by the same user, albeit consisting of one or two sentences each, suggest that this may be a case of <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:SELFPROMOTE" title="Wikipedia:SELFPROMOTE" class="mw-redirect">WP:SELFPROMOTE</a>. <a href="/wiki/User:Parishan" title="User:Parishan">Parishan</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Parishan" title="User talk:Parishan">talk</a>) 06:12, 20 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
</ol>

<li><b>Keep</b> Many Islamic Turks were expelled from Georgia and resettled in Azerbaijani by the Soviets, including ethnic cleansing. Dashgyn is an Georgian/Azerbaijani Turk who has held many political positions within that community but it's difficult to gauge the importance of these groups without local knowledge. However he was founder and President of the Georgian Azerbaijanis National Assembly from 2002 to 2011, as confirmed <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.news.az/articles/50947">here</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.eurasianet.org/departments/news/articles/eav031209c.shtml">here</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.turkishweekly.net/news/86255/asd.html">here</a>, and <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.google.com/search?q=Georgian+Azerbaijanis+National+Assembly">so on</a>; the organization appears to be a significant representative of the Georgian/Azerbaijani Turks. Dashgyn would pass <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:POLITICIAN" title="Wikipedia:POLITICIAN" class="mw-redirect">WP:POLITICIAN</a> #1 and/or #2. It's a good catch on the nom's part, but not concerned about <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:COI" title="Wikipedia:COI" class="mw-redirect">WP:COI</a>, if there is specific content that is inappropriate for Wikipedia it should be removed, but the existential question if we should have an article on this person I believe would be keep. -- <a href="/wiki/User:Green_Cardamom" title="User:Green Cardamom">Green Cardamom</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Green_Cardamom" title="User talk:Green Cardamom">talk</a>) 18:50, 20 August 2013 (UTC)</li>

<li>Well the person exists, but I still can't see any notability. The article lists 12 books, 12 footnotes, and 12 external links. The same user has published it in over 20 Wikipedias. (It is <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://toolserver.org/~luxo/contributions/contributions.php?user=Robert+Desjardins">his only contribution to Wikipedia</a>.) Compare this with the result of your research and you have a world famous author on the one side and an unknown young poet, that have published a few texts in Spanish on the other. --<a href="/wiki/User:Martssnail" title="User:Martssnail">Martssnail</a> (<a href="/w/index.php?title=User_talk:Martssnail&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User talk:Martssnail (page does not exist)">talk</a>) 17:30, 20 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
<li><b>Keep</b> There are many articles both <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.google.com/search?q=%22Sergio+Esteban+V%C3%A9lez%22+site%3Aelmundo.com">by and about Sergio</a> in <i>El Mundo</i>. Not sure when Sergio began working at <i>El Mundo</i> but most likely some of this articles predate his position there because this <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.elmundo.com/portal/resultados/detalles/?idx=160048">El Mundo article</a> says "Formerly known as the Child Poet, Velez, <i>from an early age, has been prominent in the city</i> as an important cultural landmark" and "now recognized not only within the country but also abroad," confirmed by the other sources linked by Vejvančický he has won numerous international poetry awards both in Colombia and abroad (the USA and Canada). There are other Colombian newspapers <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.google.com/search?q=%22Sergio+Esteban+Vélez%22+site%3Aelcolombiano.com"><i>El Colombiano</i></a> and <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.google.com/search?q=%22Sergio+Esteban+Vélez%22+site%3Aelespectador.com"><i>El Espectador</i></a> - about 130 results, I have not gone through them but my sense is someone doesn't win all these awards internationally, have so many mentions in multiple Colombian newspapers, without being a notable poet, a profession not known for this sort of attention at a young age. The Spanish AfD was 4 years ago before some of these sources and awards. -- <a href="/wiki/User:Green_Cardamom" title="User:Green Cardamom">Green Cardamom</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Green_Cardamom" title="User talk:Green Cardamom">talk</a>) 18:07, 20 August 2013 (UTC)</li>

<li><img alt="Pictogram voting comment.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a6/Pictogram_voting_comment.svg/15px-Pictogram_voting_comment.svg.png" width="15" height="15" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a6/Pictogram_voting_comment.svg/23px-Pictogram_voting_comment.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a6/Pictogram_voting_comment.svg/30px-Pictogram_voting_comment.svg.png 2x" />&#160;<b>Comment</b> There may be arguments for keeping this, but I expect it is similar to the first (deleted) version and could conceivably be speedied as recreation of a page deleted per a discussion - have we considered that? <a href="/wiki/User:Cathfolant" title="User:Cathfolant">Cathfolant</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Cathfolant" title="User talk:Cathfolant">talk</a>) 16:44, 26 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
<li><img alt="Pictogram voting comment.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a6/Pictogram_voting_comment.svg/15px-Pictogram_voting_comment.svg.png" width="15" height="15" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a6/Pictogram_voting_comment.svg/23px-Pictogram_voting_comment.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a6/Pictogram_voting_comment.svg/30px-Pictogram_voting_comment.svg.png 2x" />&#160;<b>Comment</b> The deletion discussions <a href="//la.wikipedia.org/wiki/Disputatio_Vicipaediae:Propaganda#Sergius_Stephanus_Velez" class="extiw" title="la:Disputatio Vicipaediae:Propaganda">here</a> (and <a href="//br.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Kumuniezh/An_davarn/sizhunvezh_42,_bloaz_2010#Sergio_Esteban_V.C3.A9lez" class="extiw" title="br:Wikipedia:Kumuniezh/An davarn/sizhunvezh 42, bloaz 2010">here</a>, for those of you who can read Breton; I certainly can't) might prove useful. <a href="/wiki/User:Cathfolant" title="User:Cathfolant">Cathfolant</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Cathfolant" title="User talk:Cathfolant">talk</a>) 18:21, 26 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
<li><img alt="Pictogram voting comment.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a6/Pictogram_voting_comment.svg/15px-Pictogram_voting_comment.svg.png" width="15" height="15" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a6/Pictogram_voting_comment.svg/23px-Pictogram_voting_comment.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a6/Pictogram_voting_comment.svg/30px-Pictogram_voting_comment.svg.png 2x" />&#160;<b>Comment</b> I kindly want to clarify some items the user Martssnail has mentioned. First of all, Vélez really won the Premio Nacional de Periodismo Simón Bolívar. The confusion is due to the fact that that award is given in different categories for various kinds of journalism. They do have prizes in different modalities: Interview, Criticism, Opinion journalism, Investigative journalism and so on. In 2010, María Elvira Samper won in the modality “All a life in journalism” and Sergio Esteban Vélez was awarded for the best interview made in Colombia in that year. It is the same as at the Oscars for films: in that competition, in the same year, there are prizes for many people in different specialties, and all they are called “Oscar winners”.</li>
</ul>
<p>I am also surprised to learn that you consider that Vélez' resume is not outstanding at all. You should take into account that he has been publishing articles in Colombian newspapers for more than ten years. Although he is still very young (29), he is columnist of one of the most important newspapers of Colombia and he has become one of the most relevant cultural journalists in Colombia. His work in the newspaper El Mundo has made of him an important voice among his people. His resume includes not only his career as a journalist, but also his trajectory as a poet. Still a boy, he had already published three poetry books and he became known as a child prodigy and well known among the intellectuals of Medellin, his city. That fame is alive still today, and regardless of the fact that he is no longer living at his country since several years ago, he continues analyzing and reviewing the important news of culture in Colombia. I have checked many other resumes of Colombian writers and journalists on Wikipedia, and I found that many of them do not show enough notability or that they have less notoriety than Sergio Esteban Vélez has. Thus, I request you to reconsider your opinions --<a href="/w/index.php?title=User:Beausejour15&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User:Beausejour15 (page does not exist)">Beausejour15</a> (<a href="/w/index.php?title=User_talk:Beausejour15&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User talk:Beausejour15 (page does not exist)">talk</a>)</p>

In the four years since 2009 in all 31 Wikipedias it was only one anonymous user, now living in Canada (<a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/132.208.73.76" title="Special:Contributions/132.208.73.76">IP 132.208.73.76</a>), who wrote about this person. For Wikipedia purposes, <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:GNG" title="Wikipedia:GNG" class="mw-redirect">WP:GNG</a> says need multiple sources about the topic in depth. <li>I made this same response to you in another AFD, but it bears repeating, @<a href="/wiki/User:Laval" title="User:Laval">Laval</a>:: that this is the English language Wikipedia only means that we write it in English for English-speaking readers. There is no requirement that sources demonstrating notability be in English. <b><a href="/wiki/User:Postdlf" title="User:Postdlf">postdlf</a></b> (<i><a href="/wiki/User_talk:Postdlf" title="User talk:Postdlf">talk</a></i>) 14:55, 27 August 2013 (UTC)
<ul>
<li>If that is an official policy, then I emphatically disagree with that. As I have stated several times, and certainly bears repeating again and again, it is well within the rights of the community to impose such a requirement.
<p>Also, I would like to see the exact policy which clarifies this matter (if such a policy exists), as I would like to bring that up at some point and work towards reassessing such an incredibly flawed and incorrect policy.</p>
<p>Furthermore, as history has proven over the years, Wikipedia functions as a community-led project. The community has every right to impose any restriction so long as there is consensus to impose such restrictions. This is exactly how current policies have ultimately been formulated, as a result of discussion and debate among community members. Change is good. That bears plenty of repetition, doesn't it? <a href="/wiki/User:Laval" title="User:Laval">Laval</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Laval" title="User talk:Laval">talk</a>) 15:07, 27 August 2013 (UTC)</p>

<li>@<a href="/wiki/User:Laval" title="User:Laval">Laval</a>:, within <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:V" title="Wikipedia:V" class="mw-redirect">WP:V</a> at <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:NONENG" title="Wikipedia:NONENG" class="mw-redirect">WP:NONENG</a> ("Citations to non-English sources are allowed."), and within <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:N" title="Wikipedia:N" class="mw-redirect">WP:N</a> at <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:GNG" title="Wikipedia:GNG" class="mw-redirect">WP:GNG</a> ("Sources may encompass published works in all forms and media, and in any language"). Both exactly where you'd expect to find the issue addressed. What did you read that made you think the contrary? It's one thing to assert what you think policy should be; it's another thing to assert it as if you think it's already policy when, in fact, policy expressly says the opposite. The former is an opinion; the latter is a mistake. At any rate, <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:VPP" title="Wikipedia:VPP" class="mw-redirect">WP:VPP</a> is the place to propose such a wide-reaching change, not within individual AFD&#160;!votes, though I'd recommend you not waste your time because there is zero chance of that gaining consensus. <b><a href="/wiki/User:Postdlf" title="User:Postdlf">postdlf</a></b> (<i><a href="/wiki/User_talk:Postdlf" title="User talk:Postdlf">talk</a></i>) 15:22, 27 August 2013 (UTC)</li>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Gavin_Boyter"><a href="/wiki/Gavin_Boyter" title="Gavin Boyter">Gavin Boyter</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Gavin_Boyter&amp;action=edit&amp;section=T-1" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Gavin Boyter">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Gavin_Boyter&amp;veaction=edit&amp;section=T-1" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Gavin Boyter" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl>
<dd><span id="Gavin_Boyter"></span><span class="plainlinks nourlexpansion lx"><a href="/wiki/Gavin_Boyter" title="Gavin Boyter">Gavin Boyter</a> <tt>(</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Gavin_Boyter&amp;action=edit">edit</a><tt>|</tt><a href="/wiki/Talk:Gavin_Boyter" title="Talk:Gavin Boyter">talk</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Gavin_Boyter&amp;action=history">history</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Gavin_Boyter&amp;action=protect">protect</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Whatlinkshere/Gavin_Boyter&amp;limit=999">links</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Gavin_Boyter&amp;action=watch">watch</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;page=Gavin+Boyter">logs</a><tt>)</tt></span> – (<a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Gavin_Boyter" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Gavin Boyter">View AfD</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://toolserver.org/~snottywong/cgi-bin/votecounter.cgi?page=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Gavin_Boyter">Stats</a></span>)</dd>
<dd>(<span class="plainlinks" style=""><i>Find sources:</i>&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?as_eq=wikipedia&amp;q=%22Gavin+Boyter%22&amp;num=50">"Gavin Boyter"</a>&#160;–&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?q=%22Gavin+Boyter%22&amp;tbm=nws&amp;tbs=ar:1">news</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?tbs=bks:1&amp;q=%22Gavin+Boyter%22">books</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://scholar.google.com/scholar?q=%22Gavin+Boyter%22">scholar</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.jstor.org/action/doBasicSearch?Query=%22Gavin+Boyter%22&amp;acc=on&amp;wc=on">JSTOR</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://images.google.com/images?safe=off&amp;as_rights=(cc_publicdomain%7ccc_attribute%7ccc_sharealike%7ccc_noncommercial%7ccc_nonderived)&amp;q=%22Gavin+Boyter%22">free images</a></span>)</dd>
</dl>
<p>Appears to fail <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:CREATIVE" title="Wikipedia:CREATIVE" class="mw-redirect">WP:CREATIVE</a>. Notwithstanding Boyter's achievements, a search for references seems to indicate the subject currently fails <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:ANYBIO" title="Wikipedia:ANYBIO" class="mw-redirect">WP:ANYBIO</a>. There are also <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:PROMO" title="Wikipedia:PROMO" class="mw-redirect">WP:PROMO</a> concerns, not to mention exploitation of Wikipedia to promote <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Yuri_Gadyukin" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Yuri Gadyukin">the Yuri Gadyukin hoax</a>. Perhaps an article will be merited in the future, but for now it seems to be <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:TOOSOON" title="Wikipedia:TOOSOON" class="mw-redirect">WP:TOOSOON</a>. A redirect to the film <i><a href="/w/index.php?title=Sparks_and_Embers&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Sparks and Embers (page does not exist)">Sparks and Embers</a></i><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.cinemagine.com/sparksandembers/">[79]</a> may be valid (if notable), except that article doesn't exist. I wish you all the best in your endeavours, Mr Boyter. <span style="white-space:nowrap;">-- <a href="/wiki/User:Trevj#top" title="User:Trevj">Trevj</a></span> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Trevj#top" title="User talk:Trevj">talk</a>) 13:31, 19 August 2013 (UTC)</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Peter_D_Matthews"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Peter_D_Matthews&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Peter D Matthews (page does not exist)">Peter D Matthews</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Peter_D_Matthews&amp;action=edit&amp;section=T-1" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Peter D Matthews">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Peter_D_Matthews&amp;veaction=edit&amp;section=T-1" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Peter D Matthews" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl>
<dd><span id="Peter_D_Matthews"></span><span class="plainlinks nourlexpansion lx"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Peter_D_Matthews&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Peter D Matthews (page does not exist)">Peter D Matthews</a> <tt>(</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Peter_D_Matthews&amp;action=edit">edit</a><tt>|</tt><a href="/wiki/Talk:Peter_D_Matthews" title="Talk:Peter D Matthews">talk</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Peter_D_Matthews&amp;action=history">history</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Peter_D_Matthews&amp;action=protect">protect</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Whatlinkshere/Peter_D_Matthews&amp;limit=999">links</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Peter_D_Matthews&amp;action=watch">watch</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;page=Peter+D+Matthews">logs</a><tt>)</tt></span> – (<a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Peter_D_Matthews" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Peter D Matthews">View AfD</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://toolserver.org/~snottywong/cgi-bin/votecounter.cgi?page=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Peter_D_Matthews">Stats</a></span>)</dd>
<dd>(<span class="plainlinks" style=""><i>Find sources:</i>&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?as_eq=wikipedia&amp;q=%22Peter+D+Matthews%22&amp;num=50">"Peter D Matthews"</a>&#160;–&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?q=%22Peter+D+Matthews%22&amp;tbm=nws&amp;tbs=ar:1">news</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?tbs=bks:1&amp;q=%22Peter+D+Matthews%22">books</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://scholar.google.com/scholar?q=%22Peter+D+Matthews%22">scholar</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.jstor.org/action/doBasicSearch?Query=%22Peter+D+Matthews%22&amp;acc=on&amp;wc=on">JSTOR</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://images.google.com/images?safe=off&amp;as_rights=(cc_publicdomain%7ccc_attribute%7ccc_sharealike%7ccc_noncommercial%7ccc_nonderived)&amp;q=%22Peter+D+Matthews%22">free images</a></span>)</dd>
</dl>
<p>Non-notable fringe author known for having recently proposed yet another hypothesis for the <a href="/wiki/Shakespeare_authorship_question" title="Shakespeare authorship question">Shakespeare authorship question</a>. No secondary sources, no signs of independent coverage. (When you search for sources, don't mistake him for another "Peter Matthews" who is a well-published literary critic.) <a href="/wiki/User:Future_Perfect_at_Sunrise" title="User:Future Perfect at Sunrise">Fut.Perf.</a> <a href="/wiki/User_talk:Future_Perfect_at_Sunrise" title="User talk:Future Perfect at Sunrise">☼</a> 06:35, 18 August 2013 (UTC)</p>
<ul>
<li><b>Delete</b> Does not satisfy <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:BIO" title="Wikipedia:BIO" class="mw-redirect">WP:BIO</a> as there is no indication of independent significant coverage in reliable secondary sources. The subject appears to have worked in a field unrelated to history (<a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.petermatthews.com.au/bio.htm">[80]</a>) and the award mentioned in the article is not sufficient to establish notability. <a href="/wiki/User:Johnuniq" title="User:Johnuniq">Johnuniq</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Johnuniq" title="User talk:Johnuniq">talk</a>) 07:59, 18 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
</ul>
<p>There are 600 citations if you care to look at his book which is sold throughout the world through the most notable bookstores! The details about the author were taken directly from his bio as cited, therefore your assertions are proven false and malicious. He is a reputable doctor of philosophy and history. He is not a literary critic - you are completely mistaken. Try searching Dr Peter D Matthews in google and you will be surprised. Or search any one of his books. <small><span class="autosigned">— Preceding <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Signatures" title="Wikipedia:Signatures">unsigned</a> comment added by <a href="/wiki/User:George134" title="User:George134">George134</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:George134" title="User talk:George134">talk</a> • <a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/George134" title="Special:Contributions/George134">contribs</a>) 12:44, 18 August 2013 (UTC)</span></small></p>
<dl>
<dd><small class="delsort-notice">Note: This debate has been included in the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Deletion_sorting/Authors" title="Wikipedia:WikiProject Deletion sorting/Authors">list of Authors-related deletion discussions</a>. <a href="/wiki/User:Northamerica1000" title="User:Northamerica1000">Northamerica1000</a><sup><a href="/wiki/User_talk:Northamerica1000" title="User talk:Northamerica1000">(talk)</a></sup> 13:03, 18 August 2013 (UTC)</small></dd>
<dd><small class="delsort-notice">Note: This debate has been included in the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Deletion_sorting/Australia" title="Wikipedia:WikiProject Deletion sorting/Australia">list of Australia-related deletion discussions</a>. <a href="/wiki/User:Northamerica1000" title="User:Northamerica1000">Northamerica1000</a><sup><a href="/wiki/User_talk:Northamerica1000" title="User talk:Northamerica1000">(talk)</a></sup> 13:03, 18 August 2013 (UTC)</small></dd>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><b>Delete</b>. Mr. Matthews has not been the subject of significant coverage in multiple reliable sources (or even one, for that matter), so he does not meet <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:GNG" title="Wikipedia:GNG" class="mw-redirect">WP:GNG</a>. If/when his work receives more attention and discussion, an article would be perfectly appropriate. A side-note to the article creator: don't be offended by this; the article's subject just doesn't meet notability standards at this time. Please don't be discouraged, and keep up your work on WP. —<a href="/wiki/User:Theodore!" title="User:Theodore!">Theodore!</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Theodore!" title="User talk:Theodore!">talk</a>) (<a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/Theodore!" title="Special:Contributions/Theodore!">contribs</a>) 18:01, 18 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
<li><b>Delete</b> - self-published author whose books have received no significant coverage. --<a href="/wiki/User:NeilN" title="User:NeilN"><b><font color="#003F87">Neil<font color="#CD0000">N</font></font></b></a> <sup><font face="Calibri"><i><a href="/wiki/User_talk:NeilN" title="User talk:NeilN"><font color="#003F87">talk to me</font></a></i></font></sup> 20:12, 18 August 2013 (UTC)</li>

<li><b>I've deleted the article</b>. The creator has blanked it, and there are no other significant edits to it. I take this as a request for speedy deletion. <a href="/wiki/User:Bishonen" title="User:Bishonen">Bishonen</a> | <a href="/wiki/User_talk:Bishonen" title="User talk:Bishonen">talk</a> 22:00, 18 August 2013 (UTC).</li>
