<dd><span id="Sydney_James_Van_Pelt"></span><span class="plainlinks nourlexpansion lx"><a href="/wiki/Sydney_James_Van_Pelt" title="Sydney James Van Pelt">Sydney James Van Pelt</a> <tt>(</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Sydney_James_Van_Pelt&amp;action=edit">edit</a><tt>|</tt><a href="/wiki/Talk:Sydney_James_Van_Pelt" title="Talk:Sydney James Van Pelt">talk</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Sydney_James_Van_Pelt&amp;action=history">history</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Sydney_James_Van_Pelt&amp;action=protect">protect</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Whatlinkshere/Sydney_James_Van_Pelt&amp;limit=999">links</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Sydney_James_Van_Pelt&amp;action=watch">watch</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;page=Sydney+James+Van+Pelt">logs</a><tt>)</tt></span> – (<a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Sydney_James_Van_Pelt" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Sydney James Van Pelt">View AfD</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://toolserver.org/~snottywong/cgi-bin/votecounter.cgi?page=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Sydney_James_Van_Pelt">Stats</a></span>)</dd>
<dd>(<span class="plainlinks" style=""><i>Find sources:</i>&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?as_eq=wikipedia&amp;q=%22Sydney+James+Van+Pelt%22&amp;num=50">"Sydney James Van Pelt"</a>&#160;–&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?q=%22Sydney+James+Van+Pelt%22&amp;tbm=nws&amp;tbs=ar:1">news</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?tbs=bks:1&amp;q=%22Sydney+James+Van+Pelt%22">books</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://scholar.google.com/scholar?q=%22Sydney+James+Van+Pelt%22">scholar</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.jstor.org/action/doBasicSearch?Query=%22Sydney+James+Van+Pelt%22&amp;acc=on&amp;wc=on">JSTOR</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://images.google.com/images?safe=off&amp;as_rights=(cc_publicdomain%7ccc_attribute%7ccc_sharealike%7ccc_noncommercial%7ccc_nonderived)&amp;q=%22Sydney+James+Van+Pelt%22">free images</a></span>)</dd>

SPA editor doesn't exactly instill confidence either.<br />
This same page created across other wikis (e.g., es.wiki) isn't a good sign either.<br />

<ul>
<li><b>Keep</b> <s><small><b>Merge</b> <i><a href="/wiki/British_Journal_of_Medical_Hypnotism" title="British Journal of Medical Hypnotism">British Journal of Medical Hypnotism</a></i> and <a href="/wiki/British_Society_of_Medical_Hypnotists" title="British Society of Medical Hypnotists">British Society of Medical Hypnotists</a> into <a href="/wiki/Sydney_James_Van_Pelt" title="Sydney James Van Pelt">Sydney James Van Pelt</a>.</small></s> I know, hypnotism, but this was taken seriously for a time as a medical treatment and he helped pioneer it, according to this source.<a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.se/books?id=k-tVr09oq3IC&amp;pg=PA318">[81]</a> One of his books was reviewed in <i><a href="/wiki/The_American_Journal_of_Psychology" title="The American Journal of Psychology" class="mw-redirect">The American Journal of Psychology</a></i><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.jstor.org/stable/1419472">[82]</a>. He was called a "leading medical hypnotist" in the <i>New York Times</i> (07 Aug 1954, "Asthma Laid to Tensions"). For anyone searching most results found as "S. J. van Pelt". -- <a href="/wiki/User:Green_Cardamom" title="User:Green Cardamom">Green Cardamom</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Green_Cardamom" title="User talk:Green Cardamom">talk</a>) 05:36, 18 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
<li><b>Keep</b> Meets <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:ACADEMIC" title="Wikipedia:ACADEMIC" class="mw-redirect">WP:ACADEMIC</a> as the <a href="/wiki/Editor-in-chief" title="Editor-in-chief">editor-in-chief</a> of a notable journal. <b>Oppose merging</b> of the articles on the society and the journal into this bio, although I don't have a problem with merging the society article into the journal article (but not the other way around). --<a href="/wiki/User:Randykitty" title="User:Randykitty">Randykitty</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Randykitty" title="User talk:Randykitty">talk</a>) 13:36, 18 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dd>
<ul>
<li>How determine the journal is notable? -- <a href="/wiki/User:Green_Cardamom" title="User:Green Cardamom">Green Cardamom</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Green_Cardamom" title="User talk:Green Cardamom">talk</a>) 14:48, 18 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dd>
<ul>
<li>The journal was indexed in <a href="/wiki/MEDLINE" title="MEDLINE">MEDLINE</a>, a rather selective database and therefore meets <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:NJournals" title="Wikipedia:NJournals" class="mw-redirect">WP:NJournals</a>. --<a href="/wiki/User:Randykitty" title="User:Randykitty">Randykitty</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Randykitty" title="User talk:Randykitty">talk</a>) 17:04, 18 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dd>
<ul>
<li>It was in Medline but no longer. Some caveats about Medline in <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:NJournals" title="Wikipedia:NJournals" class="mw-redirect">WP:NJournals</a>, not an automatic notability. And only 1 year's (volume) of the journal were indexed (out of 17).<a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/nlmcatalog/9421498">[83]</a> Looks like one good source (Gravitz, Melvin (1987)). Still believe Van Pelt, his Society and his Journal would be notable as a single article, harder to justify three articles. No information would be lost combining and maintain redirects. -- <a href="/wiki/User:Green_Cardamom" title="User:Green Cardamom">Green Cardamom</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Green_Cardamom" title="User talk:Green Cardamom">talk</a>) 18:07, 18 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dd>
<ul>
<li>That remark in NJournals is because many people equate PuBMed and MEDLINE. The latter is selective, but the former contains not only MEDLINE-indexed journals, but also journals that are in <a href="/wiki/PubMed_Central" title="PubMed Central">PubMed Central</a>, which are not necessarily notable. That this journal was indexed for only 1 year is not much of a problem, I think. It's not like it was delisted by MEDLINE or something like that, indexing stopped simply because the journal folded. Both the journal and the society have histories independent of van Pelt, so I don't think that merging them there is appropriate. The histories of the journal and society, however, do overlap, so merging the society into the journal article makes most sense to me. --<a href="/wiki/User:Randykitty" title="User:Randykitty">Randykitty</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Randykitty" title="User talk:Randykitty">talk</a>) 19:29, 18 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dd>
<ul>
<li>OK good enough. I've change my vote to Keep and worry about merge elsewhere. -- <a href="/wiki/User:Green_Cardamom" title="User:Green Cardamom">Green Cardamom</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Green_Cardamom" title="User talk:Green Cardamom">talk</a>) 02:30, 19 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
</ul>
</dd>

</dd>

<p><span class="outdent-template" style="display:block; margin-top:-0.5em; color:#AAA;"><span style="display:inline-block; overflow:hidden;">┌</span><span style="display:inline-block; overflow:hidden; width:15.2em;">────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────</span><span style="display:inline-block; overflow:hidden;">┘</span></span> <b>Comment</b>, with a question: So is the idea to keep the article and improve it, then? Whether or not the answer to that is a yes, I have sincere and serious questions about having three, let alone this one article or an article composed of the three articles. For what it's worth, <a href="/wiki/Hypnotism" title="Hypnotism" class="mw-redirect">hypnotism</a> as a page is very poorly done, especially with its treatment of its medical uses, legitimacy, or efficacy.</p>
<p>Whether or not a journal is indexed by MEDLINE/PubMed/Ovid/WoK/WoS/G Scholar/whatever shouldn't in and of itself be a sign of a journal's notability or lack thereof, in the case of those that aren't indexed. However, these do roughly indicate whether a journal may be notable enough.</p>
<p>My main complaint with the <i>British Journal of Medical Hypnotism</i> is that medical libraries and other academic libraries do not carry this journal, either as hard-copy versions or e-journals. In fact, in order to determine whether this was notable, I had to go out of my way to hunt down issues of this journal. Further, this isn't a journal with any significant readership and isn't particularly well cited, even in its area of academic rigour. Its contributors do not, in fact, number that many.</p>
<p>As for Dr. van Pelt himself, his work does not seem to have lasted the test of time and he has not left enough of a legacy. van Pelt appears not have be adequately notable per the appropriate notability criteria. As an alumnus of the Sydney Medical School, he does not appear to be recorded in the School's annals, which is further suggestive of his lack of having made enough of a mark to be included on Wikipedia. --Qwerty Binary (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Qwerty_Binary" title="User talk:Qwerty Binary">talk</a>) 10:49, 23 August 2013 (UTC)</p>
<hr style="width:55%;" />

Of the three references listed, the first is impossible to evaluate, being both offline and in a foreign language; the second is a dead link; and the third does not appear to mention the subject at all that I could find. I don't doubt that he existed and so on, and I recognize the difficulty of finding sources for someone of his generation - but I need to see some supporting evidence for the notability claims like "pioneer of modern medical hypnosis and hypnotherapy". I am open to changing my opinion if verification can be found. --<a href="/wiki/User:MelanieN" title="User:MelanieN">MelanieN</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:MelanieN" title="User talk:MelanieN">talk</a>) 22:05, 26 August 2013 (UTC)</li>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Elissa_Sursara"><a href="/wiki/Elissa_Sursara" title="Elissa Sursara">Elissa Sursara</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Elissa_Sursara&amp;action=edit&amp;section=T-1" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Elissa Sursara">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Elissa_Sursara&amp;veaction=edit&amp;section=T-1" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Elissa Sursara" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl>
<dd><span id="Elissa_Sursara"></span><span class="plainlinks nourlexpansion lx"><a href="/wiki/Elissa_Sursara" title="Elissa Sursara">Elissa Sursara</a> <tt>(</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Elissa_Sursara&amp;action=edit">edit</a><tt>|</tt><a href="/wiki/Talk:Elissa_Sursara" title="Talk:Elissa Sursara">talk</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Elissa_Sursara&amp;action=history">history</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Elissa_Sursara&amp;action=protect">protect</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Whatlinkshere/Elissa_Sursara&amp;limit=999">links</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Elissa_Sursara&amp;action=watch">watch</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;page=Elissa+Sursara">logs</a><tt>)</tt></span> – (<a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Elissa_Sursara" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Elissa Sursara">View AfD</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://toolserver.org/~snottywong/cgi-bin/votecounter.cgi?page=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Elissa_Sursara">Stats</a></span>)</dd>
<dd>(<span class="plainlinks" style=""><i>Find sources:</i>&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?as_eq=wikipedia&amp;q=%22Elissa+Sursara%22&amp;num=50">"Elissa Sursara"</a>&#160;–&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?q=%22Elissa+Sursara%22&amp;tbm=nws&amp;tbs=ar:1">news</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?tbs=bks:1&amp;q=%22Elissa+Sursara%22">books</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://scholar.google.com/scholar?q=%22Elissa+Sursara%22">scholar</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.jstor.org/action/doBasicSearch?Query=%22Elissa+Sursara%22&amp;acc=on&amp;wc=on">JSTOR</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://images.google.com/images?safe=off&amp;as_rights=(cc_publicdomain%7ccc_attribute%7ccc_sharealike%7ccc_noncommercial%7ccc_nonderived)&amp;q=%22Elissa+Sursara%22">free images</a></span>)</dd>
</dl>
<p>Overly <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:NOTPROMOTION" title="Wikipedia:NOTPROMOTION" class="mw-redirect">promotional</a> BLP built on sockpuppetry and deception. It's a mess of linkspam, namedropping and notability by association.<br />
This page has <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:BOMBARD" title="Wikipedia:BOMBARD" class="mw-redirect">a lot</a> of sources but few are any good. Mostly a mix of primary sources, activist organisations and social media sites. The activist organisations are not <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:RS" title="Wikipedia:RS" class="mw-redirect">reliable sources</a> and those she has an involvement are not independent. One reliable source used is the Australian <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.theaustralian.com.au/news/nation/japanese-whaling-ship-rams-sea-shepherd-protesters/story-e6frg6nf-1226582013026">[84]</a> but that is just thrown in to to make the page look better, verifying a fact that has nothing to do with Sursara.<br />
The one reasonable <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:V" title="Wikipedia:V" class="mw-redirect">verifiable</a> source is the <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.news.com.au/technology/sci-tech/my-identity-was-stolen-over-500-times/story-fn5fsgyc-1226507440121#ixzz2c6sp47Zn">news.com.au</a> story about identity theft. That one is more an example of indentity theft than it is coverage of her and this <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:BLP1E" title="Wikipedia:BLP1E" class="mw-redirect">one event</a> is just routine <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:NOTNEWS" title="Wikipedia:NOTNEWS" class="mw-redirect">news coverage</a>. If this source is good enough to build a <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:BLP" title="Wikipedia:BLP" class="mw-redirect">BLP</a> then one would be best served by starting from scratch. The basic premise of that article is identity theft and any BLP built from it would have to primarily focus on that subject which is barely covered in this page.<br />
That one source is also used deceptively. The piece has little biographical coverage about her beyond saying she is a "Queensland conservationist' who "is an ambassador for the Australia Zoo’s Wildlife Hospital, WWF’s Earth Hour and the Sea Shepherd". In the Wikipedia page this article is used to "verify" many things. The vague claim "She is actively involved in the mediation of cruelty to animals and promotes a sustainable lifestyle." Not said in the news article. "Sursara is the ambassador for the World Wildlife Fund climate change campaign Earth Hour, for WSPA and for Australia Zoo’s Wildlife Warriors" One out of three only. "and has served as an Antarctic campaigns crew member with the organization since 2012, appearing on Animal Planet’s documentary series Whale Wars" Not said in the news article. "Sursara is considered of influence regarding environmental conservation and wildlife". Not said in the news article. "She is the ambassador for climate change campaign Earth Hour[4] by the WWF with Miranda Kerr, Peter Garrett and Mat McHugh of The Beautiful Girls, for WSPA Australia’s Humane Chain and Voices of Influence, and for Steve Irwin's Australia Zoo Wildlife Warriors program." Partialy only and does not include the namedropping. "In May 2012, Sursara collaborated with WSPA as an ambassador to their campaign to end live export, Humane Chain. ..." Not said in the news article. "Sursara is affiliated with and/or supports organizations including ....." Most organisations not mentioned in the news article. (On identity theft) "The phenomenon received considerable media attention" Wow, something right. But not really about her. "In a 2012 feature story for The Daily Telegraph, journalist Tory Shepherd revealed there were more than 500 MySpace accounts from users claiming to be Elissa Sursara during the height of her impersonations, and discussed the negative and positive impact of identity theft on Sursara's professional and personal life." Feature story? Comes close to being true but Shepard didn't reveal that number, she reported that Sursara claimed that number. This Wikipedia article is just the editors prefered puff piece with sources badly thrown in to give an appearence of being properly referenced.<br />
A search for usable coverage came up short, finding stuff by her and passing mentions. Nothing good enough for <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:GNG" title="Wikipedia:GNG" class="mw-redirect">WP:GNG</a>.<br />
She falls short as an <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:NACTORS" title="Wikipedia:NACTORS" class="mw-redirect">actor</a>. There is a lack of significant roles, lots of bit parts. While the filmography has many blue links that is just due to a sockpuppet making new pages for many of the films and those articles show no sign that the films are notable, just building a walled garden.<br />
This article was built by a series of <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:SPA" title="Wikipedia:SPA" class="mw-redirect">single purpose accounts</a> many of which have now been blocked due to sockpuppetry (<a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Sockpuppet_investigations/Thumpgoggles/Archive" title="Wikipedia:Sockpuppet investigations/Thumpgoggles/Archive">SPI</a>). Of the earlier SPAs The checkUser from the SPI notes "It is likely that there are more stale socks in the history of Elissa Sursara". These socks have brought personal vendetta into Wikipedia, turning it into a <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:BATTLEFIELD" title="Wikipedia:BATTLEFIELD" class="mw-redirect">battlefield</a> (see the SPI and <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Omar_Todd_(3rd_nomination)" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Omar Todd (3rd nomination)">Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Omar Todd (3rd nomination)</a>).<br />
Given the lack of coverage and the bad faithed gaming of the system this article should be deleted. Deny them the fruits of their abuse. Help protect the integrity of Wikipedia by keeping out spam. <a href="/wiki/User:Duffbeerforme" title="User:Duffbeerforme">duffbeerforme</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Duffbeerforme" title="User talk:Duffbeerforme">talk</a>) 09:27, 16 August 2013 (UTC)</p>

<li><b>Keep</b> I can sympathize with the nom's position, the clear history of sock puppetry and SPA is a breach of ethics that will blackmark this Wikipedia article for a lifetime. However, I can't get past certain things that show notability:
<ol>
<li>News.co.au calls her "high-profile".<a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.news.com.au/technology/sci-tech/my-identity-was-stolen-over-500-times/story-fn5fsgyc-1226507440121">[85]</a> She had a feature in <i>Girlfriend</i> magazine (July 2013)<a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://elissasursara.org/wp-content/uploads/2013/07/GF07_77_80_LIFETOLDBYYOU2.jpg">[86]</a> and this interview in <i>Girl</i><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.girl.com.au/elissa-sursara-interview.htm">[87]</a>. That's three biographical pieces, enough material to write an article with, plus all the other briefer sources that add up. There's a fourth bio piece in <i><a href="/wiki/ELLE_Magazine" title="ELLE Magazine" class="mw-redirect">ELLE Magazine</a></i> according to the article but is inaccessible online.</li>
<li>She is rumored to be the new official "Face of Australia", replacing <a href="/wiki/Hugh_Jackman" title="Hugh Jackman">Hugh Jackman</a> as the promoter of Australian tourism.<a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.omfg.com.au/2013/07/19/australia-snags-elissa-sursara-to-promote-tourism/media/1162">[88]</a> A US travel expert said that "She defines Australia and everyone identifies with her" (previous link). However this is purely rumor and there is no validating source - it could be sophisticated PR planting a seed in hopes of creating grassroots support. Or it could be true, who knows, too soon to tell. I'm not using that source in the article obviously but something to watch over the next months.</li>
<li>The nom's concern about puffrey is accurate, the article needs a redo from top to bottom given its history of SPA.</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ul>

<p>Unreferenced list of mostly non-notable books, none of which are backed up with any <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:RS" title="Wikipedia:RS" class="mw-redirect">reliable sources</a> and some of which are also up for AfD. Also potentially fails <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:INDISCRIMINATE" title="Wikipedia:INDISCRIMINATE" class="mw-redirect">WP:INDISCRIMINATE</a> - 'Excessive listings of statistics'. <a href="/wiki/User:Ritchie333" title="User:Ritchie333"><font color="#7F007F"><b>Ritchie333</b></font></a> <a href="/wiki/User_talk:Ritchie333" title="User talk:Ritchie333"><font color="#7F007F"><sup>(talk)</sup></font></a> <a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/Ritchie333" title="Special:Contributions/Ritchie333"><font color="#7F007F"><sup>(cont)</sup></font></a> 09:50, 15 August 2013 (UTC)</p>

<ul>
<li><b>Comment</b> All this material can also be found on <a href="/wiki/Humayun_Azad" title="Humayun Azad">Humayun Azad</a>. Hence it should be removed from the main article or this should be deleted/redirected. I'm not sure he quite needs a separate bibliography, but it's reasonable to carry this information somewhere since almost all notable writers have some form of Wikipedia bibliography either in their main article or as a spin-out. Even if you believe some of these books do not exist, that is not grounds for deletion, only editing. --<a href="/w/index.php?title=User:Colapeninsula&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User:Colapeninsula (page does not exist)">Colapeninsula</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Colapeninsula" title="User talk:Colapeninsula">talk</a>) 11:46, 15 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dd>
<dl>
<dd>Having a list article as a content fork when an article gets too large is a good idea. Having a list of a notable author's works is also a good idea. However (and this is kind of the crux of my argument), the information still has to be <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:V" title="Wikipedia:V" class="mw-redirect">verifiable</a>, so unless and until somebody improves the list by citing each work to a <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:RS" title="Wikipedia:RS" class="mw-redirect">reliable source</a>, we should not have it. Compare and contrast with <a href="/wiki/List_of_Hammond_organs" title="List of Hammond organs">List of Hammond organs</a> - note how every single entry is sourced. <a href="/wiki/User:Ritchie333" title="User:Ritchie333"><font color="#7F007F"><b>Ritchie333</b></font></a> <a href="/wiki/User_talk:Ritchie333" title="User talk:Ritchie333"><font color="#7F007F"><sup>(talk)</sup></font></a> <a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/Ritchie333" title="Special:Contributions/Ritchie333"><font color="#7F007F"><sup>(cont)</sup></font></a> 11:56, 15 August 2013 (UTC)
<dl>
<dd>A part of his bibliography is verifiable by <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://archives.dawn.com/weekly/books/archive/030615/books6.htm">this</a> reliable source (<a href="/wiki/Dawn_(newspaper)" title="Dawn (newspaper)">Dawn</a>). I'm sure it is possible to find out more. --<a href="/wiki/User:Vejvan%C4%8Dick%C3%BD" title="User:Vejvančický" class="mw-redirect">Vejvančický</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Vejvan%C4%8Dick%C3%BD" title="User talk:Vejvančický">talk</a> / <a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/Vejvan%C4%8Dick%C3%BD" title="Special:Contributions/Vejvančický">contribs</a>) 13:48, 15 August 2013 (UTC)
<dl>
<dd>That partially addresses the verifiability issue, but I'm not sure it addresses the issue of being an inappropriate content fork. The current revision of <a href="/wiki/Humayun_Azad" title="Humayun Azad">Humayun Azad</a> is 17,885 bytes, of which 5527 (824 words) is prose. As <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:SIZERULE" title="Wikipedia:SIZERULE" class="mw-redirect">a general rule of thumb</a>, you probably want to be looking an article size of at least double that to think about having a bibliography as a content fork. To give a comparable example, <a href="/wiki/Salman_Rushdie" title="Salman Rushdie">Salman Rushdie</a> is on 55K, has several content splits, but his bibliography is not one of them and listed in the main article. <a href="/wiki/User:Ritchie333" title="User:Ritchie333"><font color="#7F007F"><b>Ritchie333</b></font></a> <a href="/wiki/User_talk:Ritchie333" title="User talk:Ritchie333"><font color="#7F007F"><sup>(talk)</sup></font></a> <a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/Ritchie333" title="Special:Contributions/Ritchie333"><font color="#7F007F"><sup>(cont)</sup></font></a> 14:17, 15 August 2013 (UTC)
<dl>
<dd>How can be a list of works of a notable writer inappropriate content fork? The bibliography could be redirected and merged to <a href="/wiki/Humayun_Azad" title="Humayun Azad">Humayun Azad</a> but we should not delete it. Btw, I know that the recent AfD noms regarding Humayun Azad are affected by <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:ANI#Suspicious.2Fproblematic_behavior_of_Moheen_Reeyad.2C_TilottamaTitlee.2C_and_Leelabratee" title="Wikipedia:ANI" class="mw-redirect">this ANI thread</a>. --<a href="/wiki/User:Vejvan%C4%8Dick%C3%BD" title="User:Vejvančický" class="mw-redirect">Vejvančický</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Vejvan%C4%8Dick%C3%BD" title="User talk:Vejvančický">talk</a> / <a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/Vejvan%C4%8Dick%C3%BD" title="Special:Contributions/Vejvančický">contribs</a>) 14:55, 15 August 2013 (UTC)
<dl>
<dd>Generally, I feel a merge / redirect is only appropriate if you think somebody's likely to type the name into the search box, and I tend to find "'x' bibliography", "'x' discography" or "list of 'x'" works aren't. And I'd say the same regardless of who's appeared on ANI recently, as I made this identical argument before (<a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/List_of_weddings_on_The_Bold_and_the_Beautiful" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/List of weddings on The Bold and the Beautiful">example 1</a>, <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/List_of_UK_Singles_Chart_Christmas_number_twos" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/List of UK Singles Chart Christmas number twos">example 2</a>) regardless of who happened to create the article in the first place. I'll admit I was a bit harsh about saying "non-notable" when I probably actually meant "not currently verified". Let's see what other people have to say on the issue now. <a href="/wiki/User:Ritchie333" title="User:Ritchie333"><font color="#7F007F"><b>Ritchie333</b></font></a> <a href="/wiki/User_talk:Ritchie333" title="User talk:Ritchie333"><font color="#7F007F"><sup>(talk)</sup></font></a> <a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/Ritchie333" title="Special:Contributions/Ritchie333"><font color="#7F007F"><sup>(cont)</sup></font></a> 15:12, 15 August 2013 (UTC)</dd>
</dl>
</dd>
</dl>
</dd>
</dl>
</dd>

Merge into the author page. -- <a href="/wiki/User:Green_Cardamom" title="User:Green Cardamom">Green Cardamom</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Green_Cardamom" title="User talk:Green Cardamom">talk</a>) 18:03, 16 August 2013 (UTC)</li>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Jason_Cruise"><a href="/wiki/Jason_Cruise" title="Jason Cruise">Jason Cruise</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Jason_Cruise&amp;action=edit&amp;section=T-1" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Jason Cruise">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Jason_Cruise&amp;veaction=edit&amp;section=T-1" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Jason Cruise" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl>
<dd><span id="Jason_Cruise"></span><span class="plainlinks nourlexpansion lx"><a href="/wiki/Jason_Cruise" title="Jason Cruise">Jason Cruise</a> <tt>(</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Jason_Cruise&amp;action=edit">edit</a><tt>|</tt><a href="/w/index.php?title=Talk:Jason_Cruise&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Talk:Jason Cruise (page does not exist)">talk</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Jason_Cruise&amp;action=history">history</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Jason_Cruise&amp;action=protect">protect</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Whatlinkshere/Jason_Cruise&amp;limit=999">links</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Jason_Cruise&amp;action=watch">watch</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;page=Jason+Cruise">logs</a><tt>)</tt></span> – (<a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Jason_Cruise" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Jason Cruise">View AfD</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://toolserver.org/~snottywong/cgi-bin/votecounter.cgi?page=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Jason_Cruise">Stats</a></span>)</dd>
<dd>(<span class="plainlinks" style=""><i>Find sources:</i>&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?as_eq=wikipedia&amp;q=%22Jason+Cruise%22&amp;num=50">"Jason Cruise"</a>&#160;–&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?q=%22Jason+Cruise%22&amp;tbm=nws&amp;tbs=ar:1">news</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?tbs=bks:1&amp;q=%22Jason+Cruise%22">books</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://scholar.google.com/scholar?q=%22Jason+Cruise%22">scholar</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.jstor.org/action/doBasicSearch?Query=%22Jason+Cruise%22&amp;acc=on&amp;wc=on">JSTOR</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://images.google.com/images?safe=off&amp;as_rights=(cc_publicdomain%7ccc_attribute%7ccc_sharealike%7ccc_noncommercial%7ccc_nonderived)&amp;q=%22Jason+Cruise%22">free images</a></span>)</dd>
</dl>
<p>Autobiographical article. See: <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:NOTFACEBOOK" title="Wikipedia:NOTFACEBOOK" class="mw-redirect">WP:NOTFACEBOOK</a> Subject's notability is not well established by sources independent of the subject. <a href="/wiki/User:Cyphoidbomb" title="User:Cyphoidbomb">Cyphoidbomb</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Cyphoidbomb" title="User talk:Cyphoidbomb">talk</a>) 17:10, 14 August 2013 (UTC)</p>
<dl>
<dd><small class="delsort-notice">Note: This debate has been included in the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Deletion_sorting/United_States_of_America" title="Wikipedia:WikiProject Deletion sorting/United States of America">list of United States of America-related deletion discussions</a>. <a href="/wiki/User:Gene93k" title="User:Gene93k">• Gene93k</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Gene93k" title="User talk:Gene93k">talk</a>) 17:13, 14 August 2013 (UTC)</small></dd>
<dd><small class="delsort-notice">Note: This debate has been included in the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Deletion_sorting/Christianity" title="Wikipedia:WikiProject Deletion sorting/Christianity">list of Christianity-related deletion discussions</a>. <a href="/wiki/User:Gene93k" title="User:Gene93k">• Gene93k</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Gene93k" title="User talk:Gene93k">talk</a>) 17:13, 14 August 2013 (UTC)</small></dd>
<dd><small class="delsort-notice">Note: This debate has been included in the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Deletion_sorting/Authors" title="Wikipedia:WikiProject Deletion sorting/Authors">list of Authors-related deletion discussions</a>. <a href="/wiki/User:Gene93k" title="User:Gene93k">• Gene93k</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Gene93k" title="User talk:Gene93k">talk</a>) 17:13, 14 August 2013 (UTC)</small></dd>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><b>Delete</b>. There are just enough assertions of notability to where this can't be speedied, but in the end the guy just isn't notable enough for his own entry. After I trimmed down the article and found one actual non-primary and non-merchant source, I just wasn't able to find anything to show notability for him, at least not enough to warrant his own article. <a href="/wiki/User:Tokyogirl79" title="User:Tokyogirl79">Tokyogirl79</a> <a href="/wiki/User_talk:Tokyogirl79" title="User talk:Tokyogirl79"><b><span style="color: #19197;background-color: #FFFFFF;">(｡◕‿◕｡)</span></b></a> 04:10, 15 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
<li><b>Keep</b>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.sbcbaptistpress.org/bpnews.asp?ID=23317">Here</a> is a second reliable secondary source, which means he scrapes in on <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:GNG" title="Wikipedia:GNG" class="mw-redirect">WP:GNG</a>. <a href="/wiki/User:StAnselm" title="User:StAnselm"><b>St</b></a><a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/StAnselm" title="Special:Contributions/StAnselm">Anselm</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:StAnselm" title="User talk:StAnselm">talk</a>) 05:20, 15 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dd>
<ul>
<li>We need more than two news articles to show notability. The only time that 1-2 or even 3-4 sources will be enough would be if they were asserting something so overwhelmingly notable (such as him winning a Dove Award) that the article would be kept on that basis alone. The problem here is that the the third source on the article is a <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:PRIMARY" title="Wikipedia:PRIMARY" class="mw-redirect">WP:PRIMARY</a> source written by Cruise or by someone he paid to write it for him. I'm also somewhat worried about the Baptist Press source, as you'd have to prove that Cruise isn't a member of the Southern Baptist Convention. If he's a part of that group then the source would be considered more of a primary source than anything else. <a href="/wiki/User:Tokyogirl79" title="User:Tokyogirl79">Tokyogirl79</a> <a href="/wiki/User_talk:Tokyogirl79" title="User talk:Tokyogirl79"><b><span style="color: #19197;background-color: #FFFFFF;">(｡◕‿◕｡)</span></b></a> 04:09, 16 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
</ul>
</dd>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><b>Delete</b> - reliable journalistic coverage seems thin on the ground, basically comprising of the article in Baptist Press which is partically devoted to him. I can't find any relaible reviews of any of his books either. <a href="/wiki/User:Sionk" title="User:Sionk">Sionk</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Sionk" title="User talk:Sionk">talk</a>) 20:32, 15 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
<li><b>Comment</b>: Yup, he's affiliated with the SBC. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.bpnews.net/printerfriendly.asp?ID=23318">This article</a> remarks that one of Cruise's books was published by "B&amp;H Publishing Group, the trade books division of LifeWay Christian Resources of the Southern Baptist Convention". Since Baptist Press is the official paper of the SBC, that means that any article they write about him would be considered a primary source since it's in their best interest to write about him since they are publishing his product. So we're pretty much left with just one source, which isn't enough for notability. <a href="/wiki/User:Tokyogirl79" title="User:Tokyogirl79">Tokyogirl79</a> <a href="/wiki/User_talk:Tokyogirl79" title="User talk:Tokyogirl79"><b><span style="color: #19197;background-color: #FFFFFF;">(｡◕‿◕｡)</span></b></a> 04:17, 16 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
<li><b>Comment</b>
<ul>
<li>He has a quote in the <i><a href="/wiki/New_York_Times" title="New York Times" class="mw-redirect">New York Times</a></i>, reprinted from the Joelton Journal. Citation: Emily Yellin, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2000/03/26/us/joelton-journal-an-evangelical-group-for-hunters.html">"Joelton Journal: An Evangelical Group for Hunters"</a>, March 23, 2000. Last couple paragraphs.</li>
<li>Another source: "BRIEF: Church blesses the annual hunt", <i>Northeast Mississippi Daily Journal</i> (Tupelo, MS), Nov 14, 2009, Quote: "The church will have a 'turkey shoot' Saturday night. Sunday is 'camo day.' This year's guest speaker is Jason Cruise, a Franklin, Tenn., resident and founder of the Outdoor Ministry Network which works with the Tennessee Baptist Convention to teach pastors and others how to reach men who love to hunt and fish." (From database: Newspaper Source Plus, EBSCOHost).</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>With the <i>The Tennessean</i> it points to some notability as an evangelical Christian sportsman (hunter). These are brief but reliable, a couple more sources I'd vote keep. -- <a href="/wiki/User:Green_Cardamom" title="User:Green Cardamom">Green Cardamom</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Green_Cardamom" title="User talk:Green Cardamom">talk</a>) 17:54, 16 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
</ul>

<dd><small>Please add new comments below this notice. Thanks, <font face="MV Boli"><a href="/wiki/User:Dusti" title="User:Dusti"><b><font color="#FF0000">D</font><font color="#FF6600">u</font><font color="#009900">s</font><font color="#0000FF">t</font><font color="#6600CC">i</font></b></a><a href="/wiki/User_talk:Dusti" title="User talk:Dusti"><sup>*Let's talk!*</sup></a></font> 14:59, 21 August 2013 (UTC)</small></dd>
</dl>
<hr style="width:55%;" />
<ul>
<li><b>Delete</b> Very clearly not notable. Worldcat shows of the two books he wrote, one is in 19 libraries, and the other in 22. <a href="/wiki/User:DGG_(NYPL)" title="User:DGG (NYPL)">'DGG (at NYPL)</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:DGG_(NYPL)" title="User talk:DGG (NYPL)">talk</a>) 20:54, 21 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
<li><b>Comment</b>: The problem with the quote at <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2000/03/26/us/joelton-journal-an-evangelical-group-for-hunters.html?pagewanted=all&amp;src=pm">the NYT source</a> is that quotes aren't considered to be something that could show notability since most of the time they're getting quoted on something else and aren't the subject of the article in question. They've always been considered trivial sources for as long as I've been here, as someone can get quoted a hundred times yet never get any actual in-depth coverage. It means that he might be considered a reliable source on Christian/Evengelical hunters, but that's not something that gives notability. <a href="/wiki/User:Tokyogirl79" title="User:Tokyogirl79">Tokyogirl79</a> <a href="/wiki/User_talk:Tokyogirl79" title="User talk:Tokyogirl79"><b><span style="color: #19197;background-color: #FFFFFF;">(｡◕‿◕｡)</span></b></a> 06:06, 22 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
<li><b>Delete</b> -- I do not think he has yet done enough to be notable. <a href="/wiki/User:Peterkingiron" title="User:Peterkingiron">Peterkingiron</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Peterkingiron" title="User talk:Peterkingiron">talk</a>) 13:56, 22 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
<li><b>Delete</b>; not notable. Ashbeckjonathan 22:34, 25 August 2013 (UTC)</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Gerald_Imber"><a href="/wiki/Gerald_Imber" title="Gerald Imber">Gerald Imber</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Gerald_Imber&amp;action=edit&amp;section=T-1" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Gerald Imber">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Gerald_Imber&amp;veaction=edit&amp;section=T-1" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Gerald Imber" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl>
<dd><span id="Gerald_Imber"></span><span class="plainlinks nourlexpansion lx"><a href="/wiki/Gerald_Imber" title="Gerald Imber">Gerald Imber</a> <tt>(</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Gerald_Imber&amp;action=edit">edit</a><tt>|</tt><a href="/wiki/Talk:Gerald_Imber" title="Talk:Gerald Imber">talk</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Gerald_Imber&amp;action=history">history</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Gerald_Imber&amp;action=protect">protect</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Whatlinkshere/Gerald_Imber&amp;limit=999">links</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Gerald_Imber&amp;action=watch">watch</a><tt>|</tt><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;page=Gerald+Imber">logs</a><tt>)</tt></span> – (<a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Gerald_Imber" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Gerald Imber">View AfD</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://toolserver.org/~snottywong/cgi-bin/votecounter.cgi?page=Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Gerald_Imber">Stats</a></span>)</dd>
<dd>(<span class="plainlinks" style=""><i>Find sources:</i>&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?as_eq=wikipedia&amp;q=%22Gerald+Imber%22&amp;num=50">"Gerald Imber"</a>&#160;–&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?q=%22Gerald+Imber%22&amp;tbm=nws&amp;tbs=ar:1">news</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/search?tbs=bks:1&amp;q=%22Gerald+Imber%22">books</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://scholar.google.com/scholar?q=%22Gerald+Imber%22">scholar</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.jstor.org/action/doBasicSearch?Query=%22Gerald+Imber%22&amp;acc=on&amp;wc=on">JSTOR</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://images.google.com/images?safe=off&amp;as_rights=(cc_publicdomain%7ccc_attribute%7ccc_sharealike%7ccc_noncommercial%7ccc_nonderived)&amp;q=%22Gerald+Imber%22">free images</a></span>)</dd>

<p>Highly promotional article for borderline notable physician. sourced mainly to promotional interviews he has given. Possibility of notability as an author, but the article would need to be entirely rewritten. <b><a href="/wiki/User:DGG" title="User:DGG">DGG</a></b> ( <a href="/wiki/User_talk:DGG" title="User talk:DGG">talk</a> ) 02:28, 6 August 2013 (UTC)</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Tools">Tools</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:WikiProject_Biography/Arts_and_entertainment&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Tools">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:WikiProject_Biography/Arts_and_entertainment&amp;veaction=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Tools" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<dl>
<dd><i>Main tool page: <a href="//toolserver.org/%7Edispenser/view/Tools" class="extiw" title="tools:~dispenser/view/Tools">toolserver.org</a></i></dd>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="//toolserver.org/%7Edispenser/view/Reflinks" class="extiw" title="tools:~dispenser/view/Reflinks">Reflinks</a> - Edits bare references - adds title/dates etc. to bare references</li>
<li><a href="//toolserver.org/%7Edispenser/view/Checklinks" class="extiw" title="tools:~dispenser/view/Checklinks">Checklinks</a> - Edit and repair external links</li>
<li><a href="//toolserver.org/%7Edispenser/view/Dab_solver" class="extiw" title="tools:~dispenser/view/Dab solver">Dab solver</a> - Quickly resolve ambiguous links.</li>
<li><a href="//toolserver.org/%7Edispenser/view/Peer_reviewer" class="extiw" title="tools:~dispenser/view/Peer reviewer">Peer reviewer</a> - Provides hints and suggestion to improving articles.</li>
</ul>
